Absolutely No Troops Sent to Breach Lanfeng Embankment

Also Telegraphs Shandong and Henan to Inquire if There Are Malicious Agitators. Hua County Flood Losses Exceed Thirty Million

Kaifeng dispatch: Since the beginning of the month when Wen County first suffered from the Yellow River floods, followed by the emergency in Heigang and the breach at Lanfeng, nearly three weeks have passed. Kaifeng has been almost entirely surrounded by the sounds of the Yellow River. Recently, the dangerous conditions have stabilized somewhat, and people are feeling more at ease. However, on August 26th, the provincial government suddenly released a telegram from Gansu reporting a rise of four meters in the water level, causing the relaxed atmosphere to become tense again. People greet each other by inquiring about the rise and fall of the water, creating an atmosphere of fear.

Xu Xinwu, a member of the Yellow River Conservancy Committee, arrived in Kaifeng on the afternoon of the 28th, accompanied by engineer Cai Lianggong and deputy engineer Qi Hongyou. According to Xu, their tasks in the lower reaches can be divided into four categories: (A) sealing breaches, (B) adjusting and repairing dikes, (C) reinforcing embankments, and (D) assisting. The flood control efforts in the lower reaches of the Yellow River are divided into three zones. The first zone is Lanfeng, where the engineering office is located, with Chen Ruzhen, director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, as the director and Cai Lianggong as the engineer. The second zone is Changyuan, and the third zone is Heze. Materials and labor will be sourced locally, with purchases from other areas if necessary. Labor will be recruited from the affected provinces, with wages provided by the office. They have sufficient funds for the work.

The representatives from eighteen counties in western Shandong, including Han Jifu, recently issued a telegram reporting to the central government that Liu Zhi sent troops to breach the Lanfeng embankment, flooding western Shandong. Liu was furious upon reading this report. He immediately telegraphed Han Fuju, asking if there were any malicious agitators, and also sent a telegram to the central government, requesting an immediate investigation. The provincial Kuomintang headquarters also responded to Liu's telegram, sending telegrams to Chairman Lin, President Wang, President Yu, President Sun, President Ju, the Yellow River Conservancy Committee, and Chiang Kai-shek at Kuling, requesting a thorough and strict investigation.

The flood damage in Hua County is extremely severe. The provincial disaster relief committee sent a telegram yesterday to the National Government, Commander-in-Chief Chiang, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, the Disaster Relief Committee, and various charitable organizations in the north and south, stating: "According to a telegram from the Hua County Flood Relief Association, Chairman Zhang Jun of the Henan Provincial Disaster Relief Committee, the Yellow River breach has caused devastating floods, inundating Hua County. The county government and various organizations have already reported this by telegram. We are now providing a detailed account of the actual situation based on our investigation: On August 3rd,姬兆豐 Ji Zhaofeng, a bandit leader from Changyuan County, and Zhai Xuewen, a squad leader, successively breached the west bank of the Yellow River, flooding over 600 villages in Hua County. Over 400 villages have been completely submerged. The water covers over 5,000 square li and is 3 to over 10 feet deep. The loss of autumn crops is estimated at 1,500 yuan per square li, totaling over 8 million yuan. Over 450,000 houses have collapsed, estimated at 30 yuan each, totaling over 13 million yuan. Approximately 15,000 livestock have drowned, estimated at 50 yuan each, totaling over 750,000 yuan. The loss of property, such as stored grain, clothing, and miscellaneous items, is estimated at over 10 million yuan. The total loss is over 31 million yuan. Hua County is a poor and barren area with no boats prepared for such an event. People were drowning while still holding their children, or the elderly and young were carrying each other. Corpses are floating everywhere, creating a scene of extreme tragedy. Those who survived by climbing trees or rooftops were exposed to the sun and rain, suffering from hunger and cold, crying for help with no response, voices hoarse, and dying every day. It is unbearable to witness. Our fellow countrymen are almost entirely destitute. Although the local government and various charities have donated funds, and Chairman Liu has sent Director Wan with 2,000 yuan for relief, it is like a drop in the ocean. The disaster victims are struggling to survive, let alone pay taxes. We implore you to provide urgent relief and tax exemptions to save the people and show compassion for their lives. We eagerly await your response." (August 29th)

River Breaches in Southwest Shandong 91

The Zhu River and Wanfu River Are Full

Jinan Dispatch: In the southwestern part of this province, the Zhu River, Wanfu River, Zhao River, and Bali River have all experienced significant water level increases due to the Yellow River breach, causing the Yellow River water to flow into these rivers. The water level in the Zhu River and Wanfu River is now level with the banks, posing an imminent danger. The Zhao River and Bali River have both breached, resulting in flooding. The Department of Construction received a telegram yesterday from Zhang Shixie, director of the Yanzhou-Caozhou Railway Bureau, reporting that the Zhao River has breached in Jiaxiang. The department also received a telegram from Huang Baogan, a technician, from Chengwu, stating that the Bali River has breached upstream in Chengwu. The details are as follows: (1) Huang Baogan's telegram states: "Upon investigation, the Bali River has breached upstream in the Gaodingji southwest and Nanguan Beibei areas of Chengwu, flowing into the Danxian area between the Ba River and Le River. The water from the Ba River and Le River overflows into the Jinxiang area via the north bank of the Lecheng River. Last year, when Chengwu was dredging the upper reaches of the Bali River, residents opposed the project in the Nanguan Beibei section, preventing its completion. As a result, the river overflows during heavy rains. Although efforts have been made to fill the gaps in the unfinished section after the Ba River and Le River flooded in Danxian, the dikes in the sections where work has not yet begun are too low and have all overflowed. We have already reported this in a telegram. Once the Ba River and Le River projects are completed, Chengwu will repair the upper reaches, ensuring that the two rivers are protected from flooding forever." (2) Zhang Shixie's telegram states: "According to reports from the Jiaxiang stationmaster, the Zhao River has breached, causing flooding. The east, west, and south city gates are all flooded, and the roads west of the city are completely submerged. According to reports from the Jinxiang stationmaster, the water level in the Changtan River has risen by two feet and continues to rise. I respectfully report this via telegram."

The Department of Construction has dispatched special investigators to various areas to understand the extent of the flooding, the source and path of the water, the elevation of the land, and the accumulation of water. This is purely an engineering investigation to serve as the basis for future water management and river dredging. The investigators and their assigned areas are as follows: (1) Li Zhongxuan is assigned to Cao County, Heze, Dan County, and Jinxiang. (2) Li Xiangzhen is responsible for Pu County, Fan County, Yanggu, and part of Shou County. (3) Li Runfang is responsible for Dongping, Dong'a, Pingyin, and part of Shou County. All of these individuals have already departed. (August 30th)

Guangdong Province Plans Jiangqin Railway Construction 93

From Jiangmen to Qinzhou, Over Nine Hundred Li in Length

Costing Over Seventy Million, Completion in Four Years

Guangzhou dispatch: To improve transportation among the southwestern provinces, plans were previously made to build railways in Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, Guizhou, and Sichuan. However, due to the massive scale of the project and the difficulty in raising funds, construction could not begin immediately. Recently, the authorities in Guangdong and Guangxi proposed building the Qinyong Railway first, connecting Qinzhou in the southern part of Guangdong Province directly to Nanning in Guangxi Province. However, Qinzhou is located in the southern part of Guangdong Province, and access to Qinzhou from the provincial capital relies on ships, as land routes are not yet connected, making transportation inconvenient. Recently, the Guangdong Department of Construction, to improve transportation between Guangzhou and the southern part of the province, decided to first build the Jiangqin Railway, connecting key areas in the southern part of the province. This would not only promote commerce and industry in the southern part of the province, but also connect with the future Qinyong Railway. If both railways are completed, transportation in both Guangdong and Guangxi would greatly benefit. The Jiangqin Railway construction plan and funding plan have been drafted by the Department of Construction. The route starts from Jiangmen (in Xinhui County) and runs 30 li from Jiangmen to Gongyi Pier, 100 li from Gongyi to Kaiping County, 130 li from Kaiping to Enping County, approximately 113 li from Enping to Yangchun, approximately 69 li from Yangchun to Huangtang, 61 li from Huangtang to Xinyi County, approximately 21 li from Xinyi to Shatou, approximately 178 li from Shatou to Nantang, approximately 66 li from Nantang to Shichong, 44 li from Shichong to Zhanghuang, approximately 91 li from Zhanghuang to Bailao, and approximately 91 li from Bailao to Qinzhou. The entire route from Jiangmen to Gongyi, passing through Kaiping, Enping, Chun, Xinyi, Baida, and Qinzhou, is 903 li long. The funding for the railway construction will come from annual allocations from the provincial treasury and the establishment of a railway construction committee to oversee the project and be responsible for raising funds. It is planned to be completed within four years. The first year will involve surveying and mapping, costing approximately 5.86 million yuan. The second year will involve building the roadbed, costing approximately 10.83 million yuan. The third year will involve building bridges and culverts, costing approximately 47.4 million yuan. The fourth year will involve laying tracks and building stations and car factories, costing approximately 47.4 million yuan. The total cost is estimated to be over 76.7 million yuan. (August 20th)

Corpse of Murdered Man Discovered in Qizishan 98

Qizishan in Suzhou is a famous scenic spot in Wu County. Recently, it has been a popular destination for pilgrims. Yesterday morning (31st), hikers discovered the corpse of a man in elaborate clothing in a stone crevice on the highest peak of the mountain, the Seventh Mound. The man was approximately thirty years old and was wearing a gray gauze long coat. Reactions to Harassment by Wuxi Saltpeter Bureau 99

The Huijuyuan, Jizhengxing, Gu Rongsheng, and other fireworks businesses in this county reported that the arbitrary dispatch of inspectors by the Saltpeter Branch Bureau to harass their businesses was disrupting their operations. They jointly sent a letter to the Fireworks Industry Association the other day, which forwarded the letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it forward the letter to the Saltpeter Branch Bureau, stipulating investigation methods and publicizing the regulations on search and seizure, so that they could follow them. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce immediately forwarded it to the Saltpeter Branch Bureau for consideration. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce received a reply from the Branch Bureau, stating that it was acting on orders from the general office to handle the contract and tax matters, which are collected monthly without exception. Within the Bureau's jurisdiction, users of saltpeter and sulfur must be investigated regularly, in addition to the announcements. The inspectors conduct their investigations of users once every week or five days. The investigation methods are governed by the Bureau's orders, public letters from the Public Security Bureau, and an investigation log. There is no ransacking of boxes or drawers. If anyone does not believe this, the two parties can be invited to a face-to-face meeting to clarify everything. After receiving the letter, the County Chamber of Commerce has forwarded it to the Fireworks Industry Association for their review.

Yesterday, they were transferred to the County Court. Wang Baode, Mao Jinyu, Xue Fusheng, and Lu Qingyun were detained. Prosecutor Shen, accompanied by the coroner Wang, traveled to the scene to conduct an autopsy. Hangzhou Mother's Appeal in Son's Murder Case Adjudicated 107

Yao Tao, a 53-year-old widow from Zhao Ai Village, Cixi, had three unmarried sons: Zaiyuan (22 years old), Zaixing (19 years old), and Zaichuan (16 years old). They worked diligently in farming and had accumulated some savings. Several years ago, Yao Chen divided the property among her three sons, each receiving a house. The mother lived with the second and youngest sons. Recently, the eldest son Zaiyuan suspected that the mother had subsidized the construction of a new house for the second son Zaixing, leading to frequent conflicts. Subsequently, Zaiyuan ordered Zaixing to remove a straw pile from his house, leading to a physical altercation. Zaiyuan was overpowered and injured by a wooden stick. Yao Chen led her two younger sons in pursuit, pushing Zaiyuan into the river and drowning him. His uncle, Yao Ruifu, reported the incident. The two younger sons fled. Yao Chen was sentenced to fifteen years in prison. Chen refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the provincial government. Yesterday (31st) morning, the verdict was announced, reducing the sentence to six years and eight months.

Zhu Youfu and others were brought to the scene and identified Wang Dehui as the perpetrator of the armed robbery. Wang Dehui confessed to participating in the robbery and receiving a share of the stolen goods. He was sentenced to death according to the law, which was approved by the provincial government. Local News

Chamber of Commerce Jointly Appeals to the Government to Reimpose Import Tax on Foreign Rice 112

Also Cables Guangdong Provincial Government to Jointly Advocate

The National Chamber of Commerce Joint Federation, considering that domestic grain is currently cheap, hurting farmers, while a massive amount of foreign rice is being imported, inevitably hindering sales and affecting the rural economy, yesterday telegraphed the government and the Ministries of Finance and Industry, stating (titles omitted): "The case concerns a previous letter from the Zhangpu County Chamber of Commerce in Fujian, requesting that we forward a request to reimpose a small import tax on rice. We duly telegraphed your government ministries on July XX of this year. On August 9th, we received Industry Ministry document number 1926 stating, 'We have received your telegram. Regarding whether to levy taxes on imported foreign rice, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has appealed to the ministry, and the Ministry of Finance has replied, stating, "Since the meeting convened last year, the rice-producing provinces have requested the rapid imposition of import taxes, while Guangdong, a province lacking rice, argues that taxing foreign rice would harm the people's food supply and insists on dissenting. If taxes are to be imposed, they should be specified in the import tariff. However, the current import tariff is already under review by the National Government's Legislative Yuan and has not yet been finalized." ' We have recorded the aforementioned telegram and directive and have already notified you. Now we read in the August 24th newspaper report that the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, according to a customs report, "From January to July of this year, there was a trade deficit of over 289,570,000 yuan. Food ranks first among imported goods, valued at over 75,490,000 yuan. The current cheap domestic grain hurts farmers, and such a large amount of food imports is a matter of concern for the government authorities," and the Nanjing dispatch of August 31st stated, "A person in charge of the Ministry of Railways said that freight rates for grain have been reduced separately, but so far, domestic grain has not been selling well. The key lies in the duty-free import of foreign grain, which is arbitrarily encroaching on the market, and the freight rate policy is complementary to the tariff policy. If they are combined, the effect is great; if they are separated, the effect is completely lost. Therefore, supporting domestic grain production is a major issue, especially the duty-free import of foreign rice. In addition, various miscellaneous taxes and levies in the interior are also layered upon each other, forming a major obstacle to transportation and sales." "Looking at the former, the amount of foreign grain imports accounts for the largest portion of imported goods, and the claim that domestic grain is encroached upon and sold cheaply is not false. Looking at the latter, there is no shortage of domestic grain, and there is no need to rely on foreign grain, and the statement that domestic grain is being encroached upon by foreign grain and sold cheaply is even more credible. If this continues, the imports of foreign grain will increase, the sales of domestic grain will decrease, and the price will become cheaper. Now, farmers are not only worried about the drop in grain prices but also about the difficulty of selling their crops. They are struggling to survive. If we do not find ways to help, the farmers will inevitably starve to death or find other occupations. In a few years, domestic grain may indeed be insufficient to eat, and the entire country will inevitably rely on foreign grain. The Chamber is witnessing the difficulties of the times and dares not remain silent. In addition to separately telegraphing the Guangdong Provincial Government, we jointly telegraph your government ministries for review and verification, requesting that you promptly reimpose import taxes on foreign rice and eliminate miscellaneous taxes and levies, so that we can treat both the symptoms and the root causes, and there is hope for recovery. The National Chamber of Commerce United Federation respectfully bows." The association also states that the Guangdong Provincial Government believes that after the import tax on foreign rice is reimposed, grain prices will rise, hindering the people's food supply and insists on dissenting, so it specifically telegraphed the Guangdong Provincial Government, asking it to consider the overall situation and jointly advocate reimposing the import tax on foreign rice. The original telegram states (titles omitted): "The case concerns a previous letter from the Fujian Zhangpu Chamber of Commerce, requesting that we forward a request to reimpose the import tax on foreign rice. Our association duly telegraphed the National Government's Executive Yuan, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry. In August, we received the Industry Ministry's document number 19263, stating, 'We have received your telegram, etc.' (see previous excerpts). Now we read in the August 24th newspaper report that the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, according to a customs report, (excerpts omitted) Guangdong is a province that relies on foreign rice, and there is fear that once the import tax on rice is reimposed, grain prices will rise. However, the farmers in the interior are not only worried about the drop in grain prices but also about the difficulty of selling their crops. If grain prices rise, the transportation and sales of domestic grain will inevitably be crowded. Once goods flood the market, the price increase will not be significant. Moreover, to burden the entire rural population of the country with the bankruptcy for the sake of food rice in Guangdong Province is something that benevolent people would not do. In addition to re-telegraphing the Central Government, we are telegraphing Your Excellency for review, hoping that you will abandon your prejudices, consider the overall situation, and jointly advocate reimposing the import tax on foreign rice, to alleviate the farmers' distress. The National Chamber of Commerce United Federation bows."

The finances of North China have always been difficult. Since the fierce fighting, income has sharply decreased, while expenditures have been very large due to the impact of the war. Therefore, the number of deficits is too large, so we urgently need to find a way to help. We are now planning to start with increasing revenue and reducing expenditure, finding ways to rectify finances and reduce political and military expenses." At this point, the reporter asked about the relief for the current financial difficulties in North China and whether Minister Song's so-called "appropriate solutions" referred to the widely circulated plan to issue public bonds. Huang replied, "This point was not discussed, and we will not issue public bonds." Finally, the reporter asked when he would return to Beiping. Huang said that he had not yet decided.

After American Cotton and Wheat Arrive in China 120

Will First Be Mortgaged to Shanghai Banking Circles

According to Guowen News Agency, the Chinese government borrowed 50 million yuan from the United States to purchase raw cotton and wheat for shipment to China. Song Ziwen, the Minister of Finance who is negotiating this loan, has already returned to the country. The other day, Song also said that a batch of American cotton was already en route to China. Yesterday, reporters learned from industrial circles that Song had entrusted Zhang Gongquan, president of the Bank of China, and Chen Guangfu, manager of the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, to handle the loan.

Moreover, Chen Guangfu was originally in Qingdao, attending the annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society. Previously, Song had telegraphed him, inviting him to Shanghai for talks. The so-called "handling" means that after the cotton and wheat arrive in China, they will first be mortgaged to various banks in Shanghai, and then the banks will resell them to the various factories that need them. Therefore, in the afternoon, reporters went to meet Chen Guangfu to ask him about the situation. According to Chen, "Mr. Ma Yinchu and I attended the annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society in Qingdao and only returned to Shanghai yesterday (the day before yesterday). This morning, Mr. Kong Yongzhi and I visited Minister Song for a long-overdue greeting. The American cotton and wheat issue was discussed with no results. It was a superficial conversation. In any case, there must first be a plan before there can be a solution, and only with a solution can progress be made. After today's meeting with Song, it was as if we had not discussed the matter at all. So, I really cannot speculate on how the matter will proceed or how it will be handled. Minister Song will go to Nanjing in the next few days. Although I returned to Shanghai yesterday, I still plan to go to Beiping and Tianjin soon. This trip has no special business; it is the annual routine inspection of branch operations." Subsequently, the reporter asked about the Central Government raising funds from Shanghai banking circles for flood relief in North China and the Yellow River region. Chen generally replied that he had only seen it reported in the newspapers and did not know the details.

Regarding the arrival of American cotton and wheat in China, according to sources in the cotton industry, the first batch will not arrive in Shanghai until mid-September at the earliest. Considering the purchase price in the United States and the addition of tariffs and freight after arriving in China, the price per bale will far exceed the domestic market price by about one-sixth. It is questionable how it can be sold. Not only is the price of cotton like this, but also the price of wheat shipped to China in the future will certainly not be cheaper than the domestic market price. This is indeed one of the most difficult points after the American cotton and wheat are shipped to China.

Post Office to Implement Two New Regulations Today 121

Increase Postage to Southeast Asia

Retire Elderly Postal Workers

According to Huang Naishu, Director of the Postal Administration, speaking to a reporter from the Central News Agency yesterday, regarding the issue of increasing postage rates to Southeast Asia, the post office has repeatedly sent personnel to major ports such as Guangzhou, Xiamen, and Shantou to separately explain to those involved in overseas Chinese affairs due to opposition from overseas Chinese. Understanding has been reached, so it has been decided that starting tomorrow (today), all mail sent to Southeast Asia will be affixed with sufficient postage stamps according to the new regulations: 12.5 cents for regular letters and an additional 20 cents for registered letters. According to the budget, this will increase postage revenue by 100,000 yuan per year. The dismissal of 32 elderly postal workers will also be announced tomorrow (today). Each person will receive two months' salary as a retirement bonus to show preferential treatment, which will also save 100,000 yuan in expenses per year.

The Fujian bandits and communists have been severely suppressed by the army in recent days, and the bandit army has been repelled. Not only is Fuzhou as peaceful as usual, but also Yanping has not been lost. However, foreigners, misunderstanding the truth, upon hearing of bandit alerts, use the protection of overseas Chinese as an excuse and send warships to Fujian one after another, alarming international public opinion. This is also the pain suffered by a weak country.

Japanese Navy Third Fleet Commander Minai received a telegram from the Japanese Ministry of the Navy, ordering that in addition to dispatching one cruiser and two destroyers from Sasebo directly to Fujian to prepare for the evacuation of Japanese overseas Chinese, the Third Fleet in Shanghai should also dispatch warships to Fuzhou to assist in the protection of overseas Chinese. Continued News of Labor Strike at British American Tobacco Factories 124

Workers in the Printing Department Plan to Resume Work Yesterday but Failed

The Union Petitions for Investigation into the Withdrawal of Some Workers

According to Dagong News Agency, after the workers of the British American Tobacco Company's old and new factories announced a general strike, the factory's attitude remained firm, and the situation has not been resolved. The other day, the workers in the new factory's printing department advocated resuming work, which caused a reaction from the workers in other departments, leading to internal disputes. Yesterday morning at 8:00 a.m., more than 100 workers from the printing department went to the municipal government to petition. The union submitted a petition to party and government organs requesting an investigation. The details are as follows:

Failure to Resume Work After the workers of the old and new factories announced a general strike, the more than 700 workers in the printing department of the British American Tobacco Company's second factory in Puxi also participated as a whole. Now, due to internal differences of opinion, some workers gathered the other day and advocated resuming work, which led to a reaction from other workers. The workers in the printing department went to the factory as usual at 7:00 a.m. yesterday. When they were about to start working between the large rolling stone machines, the Western staff in that department prevented them from causing disturbances and incidents, so the resumption of work failed. The workers then went to the municipal government to petition for assistance.

Petitioning the Municipal Government Because of the failure to resume work, the workers in the new factory's printing department elected more than 100 representatives to cross the river to the municipal government to petition. After the municipal government received the report, it specially ordered the security team to send more than 20 patrol officers to dissuade them and instructed them to elect five representatives. The workers immediately elected Pan Quanrong and four others as representatives to visit Secretary-General Yu, requesting two points: (1) They have been idle for a long time, and their livelihood is worrying. Please order the factory to start the machines immediately. (2) Please order the Public Security Bureau to send police to protect the work. Secretary-General Yu replied, saying that the British American Tobacco Company workers had formed a legal union and should submit a petition through the union. If the union handles it improperly, more than two-thirds of the workers should submit a joint petition. The workers' petition today is not in accordance with the law, although it will be accepted, resulting in no results and a withdrawal.

Temporarily Not Mediating Yesterday, the Dagong News Agency reporter inquired with party and government organs about their attitude towards handling the British American Tobacco labor strike. According to the staff in charge, the British American Tobacco case is too complicated to resolve in a short time, and the factory's attitude is firm. Although the municipal government has drafted several solutions, it has refused to implement them, so mediation is likely to be ineffective at this time. All the pending cases have now been submitted to the municipal government for instructions and plan to temporarily not convene mediation again.

Petition for Investigation The Fifth District Cigarette Workers' Union submitted a petition to party and government organs yesterday, stating that Pan Quanrong, a worker in the rolling stone department of the new factory's printing department, has been used by the factory to preside over reactionary actions and fabricate false statements to threaten a resumption of work. They have already submitted a request for severe sanctions. Today, Pan Quanrong and others led the workers in that department into the factory to work. The entire workers, upon hearing the news, were greatly offended. The Western manager of that department, fearing conflicts that would damage the factory's machinery, refused to allow Pan Quanrong and others to start the machines. The factory then prepared two small boats, ordered Pan and others to lead more than 100 workers, including non-workers, to the municipal government to petition, with all expenses paid by the factory, and ordered Pan and others to organize a printing department union separately, hoping to sow discord and undermine unity. This illegal behavior is obviously a reactionary intention. They are willing to be the factory's lackeys.

This is clearly revealed. For this reason, Pan Quanrong's reactionary situation is continuously reported for review. It is requested that Pan Quanrong be severely sanctioned to serve as a warning, maintain the labor movement, and await orders. Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau. The Union's question to the New Voice News Agency: The workers in the new factory's printing department sent a letter to the standing committee of the union yesterday, asking them to order the Third Factory on Taopeng Road to participate in the strike, otherwise the workers in that department would resume work immediately. The original letter stated: "We heard that the representatives' meeting on the 28th produced a strike

Page 20

Committee. In the 16th year of the Republic of China, the strike for national taxes was guaranteed by the government. We have heard that there are still private workers, and after the resumption of work, our association does not have legitimate means to deal with these people. Now, the Third Factory has been established for many years, and its scope is far greater than our department. The people have always been extremely obedient to the mission of our association, so they have recently expressed their concern. We heard that your committee has people who jointly expressed their views with the Third Factory, but this has now become a bubble. Lessons can be learned from the past.

Therefore, all the workers in our department are in a state of panic and are making an inevitable request. We implore your committee to quickly express its views together with the Third Factory tomorrow morning, otherwise our department will act in accordance with the Third Factory, and our department will not be responsible for anything.

According to the petition group of the British American Tobacco Company workers, the labor strike at the British American Tobacco Company in Pudong has not been resolved for many days. Yesterday, the workers in the factory's printing department underwent another change. The details are as follows:

Detaining Representatives Because the workers' strike has caused the factory losses, the Old Jinlong Foreign Firm recruited printing workers from the Commercial Press to replace them and transferred the printing machines from the Pudong factory to the Third Factory. The workers, seeing this, were extremely panic. They sent a letter to the union, requesting to take the same steps as the Third Factory to prevent the factory from taking advantage. They elected Pan Quanrong as their representative to state their opinions and request a solution. The workers could not enter the union, but they were dissuaded by ten patrol officers from the Public Security Bureau. The workers who had reached the factory then unanimously decided to petition the municipal government for a solution. Yesterday morning at 8:00 a.m., all 600 workers in that department organized a petition group and petitioned the municipal government.

At that time, Pan Quanrong, Xu Wenqing, Chen Sihong, Zhang Xiqi, and Chen Shengkui were elected as temporary representatives and were received by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun. The workers stated their reasons, and Secretary-General Yu instructed them that the workers' willingness to resume work and their distrust of the union were their own feelings, and they could freely decide whether they needed to protest. As for the union's detention of representatives and intimidation, he would definitely investigate them strictly and had asked Public Security Bureau Chief Wen to pay attention to the security in Pudong to avoid accidents, and he gently persuaded the workers to return home. The workers were quite satisfied when they heard this.

Withdrawing from the Union Because the union could not seek benefits for the workers and the handling of the strike was improper, all 600 workers in that department withdrew from the union and will resume work today.

Cross-Border Telephone Lines in the North and South Districts to Be Removed 125

Telephone Bureau to Remove Them by the End of September

Sends Letters to Users to Apply for Reinstallation

According to Dagong News Agency, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications is now taking back all telephone lines installed by the Shanghai Telephone Company within the Chinese boundary in accordance with the temporary telephone contract in order to maintain sovereignty. The cross-border telephone lines in the South and Zhabei districts will all be removed by September 30th. The same will be done in Pudong after the branch office is established. The details are as follows:

Recovering Cross-Border Line Rights 126

According to Xu Xueyu, Director of the Telephone Bureau, speaking to a reporter from Dagong News Agency yesterday, before the temporary telephone contract was signed, the concession telephone company directly ran lines into the Chinese boundary and installed telephones, including 32 telephones in the South City District, more than 10 telephones in the Zhabei District, and more than 240 telephones in the Pudong District. The monthly rental fees, installation fees, and deposit fees for these telephones were all collected by the concession telephone company. This not only caused economic losses to our bureau but also hindered sovereignty. Now our bureau has decided to take back all the telephones installed by the Shanghai Telephone Company in the Chinese boundary or cross-border areas in accordance with the contract. We will first remove them in the North and South cities by the deadline, and the same will be done in Pudong after the branch office is established.

Cutting off Border Sky Lines 127

The sky lines of the Shanghai Telephone Company leading to the North and South cities and the submarine cables in the Huangpu River in Pudong are connected to cross-border telephones. Users in the Chinese boundary call the concession, or users in the concession call the Chinese boundary, all directly connected by the company. The Telephone Bureau has no transfer rights. After the cross-border telephones are removed, the sky lines will be cut off between the boundaries and reconnected to the distribution machine. The submarine cable in Pudong has been sold and purchased by the bureau.

User Notification Regarding Reinstallation 128

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau yesterday issued a notification to all users, which stated: Greetings. Since the signing of the temporary agreement for telephones in this city, all telephones installed by the Shanghai Telephone Company within the Chinese-controlled areas should be taken back by this Bureau immediately in order to maintain sovereignty. This Bureau now stipulates that the telephones in the concession areas of the Nanshi and Zhabei districts will be dismantled before September 30th of this year. As for the Pudong area, once a branch bureau is established, they will also be taken back according to the regulations. Regarding whether your users still need to reinstall the Bureau's telephones after the concession telephones are dismantled, please fill out the attached form and mail it to this Bureau before September 10th for review. Otherwise, if the attached form is not mailed before September 10th, this Bureau will consider that your users are willing to have the concession telephones dismantled and will not reinstall the Bureau's telephones. Therefore, this Bureau will not be responsible for any obstacles and losses incurred after the telephone dismantling. Please be informed and respond promptly. Respectfully, [signed] Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, August 31st.

Improving Switching Equipment 129

The Telephone Bureau also issued another notification to all users, which stated: Since we combined the China-Concession call fees with the monthly rental, the number of call requests per day has increased three times compared to before. The Bureau's losses are very significant. However, there are only fifty pairs of lines and only six switching seats. Therefore, we are unable to handle all the call requests promptly, and users often have to wait a long time. This is something the Bureau deeply regrets and asks for your understanding. The Bureau is currently working on expansion and adding equipment. At the same time, the Bureau hopes that your users will not abuse calls to concession telephones unless there are urgent matters, in order to reduce time and economic losses. Furthermore, if the switchboard operators are impolite to your users, please immediately inquire about their number, and report the time, your own telephone number, and the number being called to the Bureau in detail. We will handle it according to the regulations. However, the facts must be accurate, and malicious accusations should be avoided at all costs.

Cross-Border Telephone Rates 130

The Telephone Office has established the following cross-border telephone rate schedule for the Nanshi, Zhabei, and Pudong districts: (A) Trunk Lines: (I) Security Deposit: 50 yuan per pair for the Bureau; (II) Installation Fee: 20 yuan per pair for the Bureau, 10 taels per pair for the Company (collected by the Bureau on behalf); (III) Monthly Rental: 12 yuan per pair per month for the Bureau in Nanshi and Zhabei (add 2 yuan for each Bureau telephone set installed, add 1 yuan for each self-provided telephone set installed); 15 yuan per pair per month for the Bureau in Wusong, Jiangwan, and Pudong (add 2 yuan for each Bureau telephone set installed, add 1 yuan for each self-provided telephone set installed); 60 taels per pair per quarter for the Company (collected by the Bureau on behalf). (B) Special Telephone Lines: In addition to the Company's quarterly rental fee of 40 taels and 4 mace per pair and an installation fee of 10 taels per pair, all fees to be collected by the Bureau are the same as the previous item.

The China Merchants Bureau Reorganizes Shipping, Changes Supervisors, and Disputes Arise 131

It is Evident How Difficult it is to Eliminate Malpractices

Among Chinese steamships, the deepest-rooted malpractices are the comprador system, followed by the stewards and supervisors. Now, Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the China Merchants Bureau, is resolutely reforming the various bad systems of the ships one by one. On the "Puan" and "Xinming" ships, the comprador system has been abolished. The "Xinming's" steward was found to be corrupt and incited a crowd to disobey orders, and Liu forcibly removed him from the ship. Now, he has taken a further step and is changing the bad supervisors. Initially, it was a minor matter, but now it has developed into a major dispute, or perhaps this is the process that those who reorganize shipping affairs must go through.

Supervisors Neglect Their Duties On various ships, there is a position of supervisor, who is specifically responsible for the meals of the crew members. Recently, all the crew members of the "Xinjiangtian" ship reported to General Manager Liu that the food for the crew members was getting worse and worse. According to the meal expenses issued by the Bureau, they should not be eating such coarse food. This is obviously the supervisor's neglect of duty and should be changed. Other crew members on the Yangtze River ships also complained, saying that the supervisors were ineffective, resulting in the waste of money and causing intangible losses to the crew members. After receiving the report, Liu first sent someone to secretly investigate and verify the facts, and then implemented the change of supervisors.

Approval of the Change of Supervisors Liu reported this matter to the board of directors, requesting that the board of directors approve the change of supervisors of the various ships in the name of the board of directors. The board of directors believed that it was not necessary for the board of directors to approve the transfer of a supervisor. Later, they realized that this matter was seemingly small but actually large, so they immediately followed Liu's request and transferred Wang Shenggao, the supervisor of "Xinjiangtian," to serve as the supervisor of "Jiangda," and appointed Ren Tangsheng, the supervisor of "Jiangxin," to "Xinjiangtian." Fang Anquan of "Jiangda" was transferred to "Jiangxin," while Zhang Jinsheng of "Jianghua" and Fan Xinbiao of "Jiangyu" were exchanged.

Resisting Transfer After the Bureau's order was issued, Wang Gaosheng of "Xinjiangtian" was the first to disobey the order and refused to hand over, causing Ren Tangsheng to be unable to board the ship to take over. Wang Shenggao did not even go to the ship and avoided meeting. Because of his obstruction, the Bureau's order was not implemented, and all the ships were blocked. In recent days, the "Xinjiangtian" ship has been sailing without a supervisor. However, Liu is determined to implement this matter to maintain dignity and eradicate malpractices. Now, the "Xinjiangtian" ship will be suspended for repairs, and this problem should be resolved in these few days. If Wang Shenggao continues to disobey the order, Liu will take severe action.

Seamen Oppose Wang Shenggao has reported this matter to the preparatory committee of the Seamen's Union, and the Union has sent a letter to Liu Hongsheng, stating that if the Bureau can freely transfer and dismiss the supervisors based on the dissatisfaction of the crew members, then the personnel on the ships will lose the guarantee of their positions in the future. As long as a certain crew member is not satisfied, they can be arbitrarily dismissed. The Seamen's Union expressed that they could not sympathize with this matter and requested General Manager Liu to immediately withdraw the transfer order and allow the supervisors to continue in their original positions. It is heard that Liu considers the current change of supervisors of the various ships to be one of the important matters for reorganizing the internal affairs of the ships. If they resist the order or use other forces to confront the Bureau, the Bureau will submit a request to the Ministry to order the transfer in order to vigorously carry out the reorganization. Therefore, the future of this dispute is still difficult to predict.

Farmers from Caoguanjing Petitioned Party and Government Agencies Yesterday 133

To Avoid Renting Farmland at Longhua Airport

And Forward a Request to the Ministry of Transportation to Withdraw its Order

Tang Muquan and 23 other farmers from the Longhua Airport area in Caoguanjing, whose farmland near the airport was encircled by the airline, gathered more than 50 men and women and petitioned various Party and government agencies yesterday morning around 10:00 AM, requesting the authorities to order the avoidance of renting and immediately instruct the local bailiff to stop the process, and forward a request to the Ministry of Transportation to withdraw its order. The Municipal Party Headquarters sent Zhao Erchang from the Civil Training Section to receive them, who replied that he would forward the request on their behalf. The representatives of the people were satisfied and left. The original petition to the Municipal Government is as follows: Petition for avoiding the renting of farmland at Longhua Airport in Caoguanjing District, immediately ordering the local bailiff to stop the process, and forwarding a request to the Ministry of Transportation to withdraw its order. The undersigned and their families have always relied on farmland for a living. Now, an airline has filed with the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Interior to develop public air transportation, intending to expand the airport and forcibly rent the people's farmland, as evidenced by the notice issued by Yang Xinzheng, Municipal Committee Member of Caoguanjing District, on April 16th. Later, because the people submitted a document to the Party Headquarters on April 25th, complaining about the forced rental of farmland without following the procedures of the Land Law, and also petitioned your government, although there was no written reply exempting the encirclement, there was no forced process. Now, after the notice from the Land Bureau was obtained on July 26th, the people again jointly requested the Land Bureau on August 16th to exempt the rental for four reasons, and earnestly request your government to put the case on file. Now, without any approval, Lin Jizuo colluded with the local bailiff Ji Zhukang to forcibly drive wooden stakes into the people's land for encirclement and use, and wanted to forcibly dig up the people's tombs and ancestral graves. Are these methods in line with the Land Use Law? The undersigned have no choice but to petition your government to rescue the farmers, quickly order an investigation to stop it, and will be extremely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the Mayor of Shanghai Wu, by petitioners Tang Muquan, Wei Hongsheng, Zhang Jilu, Gao Lianbao, Shen Liangchen, Tang Xiuchang, Tang Chuntao, Tang Xintang, Yang Fushan, Cai Yinshan, Gao Fengming, Wang Dianchen, Shi Bosun, Hu Zhuming, Wu Amei, Hu Liansheng, Li Tangsheng, Li Liansheng, Xue Dumei, Xue Qiuyuan, Ding Qiusheng, Tang Ruifa, Zhao Huisheng.

The Representative of Sichuan's Liu (Xiang) in Shanghai Forwarded You Guocai's Telegram to He Yingqin 134

Detailed Account of the Financial Exhaustion in Guizhou Province

You Wang's troops in Guizhou have been at war for a long time. You Guocai, in order to preserve his strength, retreated to the border of Yunnan, still planning to wait for an opportunity to move. Yesterday, Deng Mingjie, the representative of Sichuan's Liu (Xiang) in Shanghai, received a telegram from You Guocai entrusted to forward to He Yingqin, which detailed the financial exhaustion in Guizhou Province and the presence of troops everywhere. I respectfully believe that my teacher is concerned about his homeland and considers going out to suppress bandits as a way to end the conflict. After reading it, I am filled with admiration and shame. I belong to the military and have always been under your guidance. It would be my sincere wish to lead my troops out and follow your lead in suppressing the Communist bandits. However, the reality is that Guizhou is full of troops. In addition to my troops and Jiang and Che's divisions, a large portion should also be transferred out to concentrate our strength and reduce the burden. Before we can move, however, we need to secure funding for deployment and regular supplies. The finances in Guizhou are more exhausted than ever before. If that is still not enough, he has added six million yuan in post-war reconstruction bonds. For Guizhou, which lives on debt, it is not possible to rashly send troops without first resolving the funding issue. Furthermore, Shao Wu [Wang Jialie] is currently advancing his troops in Tongren without stopping. If we do not first stop him, it will be difficult to discuss sending troops. My teacher is concerned about his homeland and will surely see the key to the problem and grant a solution. I await your urgent instructions. Your student, You Guocai, respectfully kowtows.

The Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association Appeals for Victims of the Yingfu Disaster 136

Three Representatives Wept and Spoke at the Red Swastika Society

The Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, due to the severe bandit disaster in Yingfu, specially appointed representatives Lü Yinnan, Ma Zhuoqing, and Wang Zhuru to take a letter to the head office of the Red Swastika Society on Danshui Road to plead for the disaster victims. The original letter is transcribed as follows: Greetings. The bandits in Fuyang, colluding with the defeated troops from Henan Province, numbering about ten thousand, have disturbed the three southwestern and eastern townships of the county and the southwestern township of Yingshang County. After being blocked by the troops, they repeatedly detoured into the territory of Fuyang, occupying the three southern, northern, and western townships of Taihe County, and also disturbed the areas of Dianji, Suji, Wang Laorenji, and Dingbei Guanjihua Ji in northern Fuyang. They burned, killed, raped, and plundered wherever they went. This association has repeatedly received telegrams from various French nationals in Fuyang and Yingshang counties, asking for help. The miserable situation is unbearable to read. It is estimated that 90% of the entire territory of Fuyang, and 50-60% of Yingshang and Taihe, have been devastated. The disaster area extends for three to four hundred miles. No less than 10,000 people have been killed, raped, and injured, or maimed. The bandits have turned villages and towns into ruins. Five to six hundred thousand disaster victims are starving. Therefore, we specially appoint representatives Lü Yinnan, Ma Zhuoqing, and Wang Zhuru to present the disaster situation. We hope that you will consider the disaster victims and urgently need help. Please quickly allocate funds to rescue them. According to the oral account of the three representatives, Lü, Ma, and Wang, the bandits set fire to houses wherever they went, and robbed both men and women, rich and poor. They tied several people together and interrogated them several times a day. Those who could not afford to redeem their tickets were immediately killed, or beaten to death with clubs, or had their scalps cut open and mercury poured in. After a while, their entire skin would peel off, and then they would be pierced with a knife. When they encountered women, if they refused to be raped, they would be beaten to death and their bodies stripped naked, with small sticks inserted into their lower parts. The bandits would clap their hands and laugh. If a young woman was holding a baby in her arms, they would snatch the baby away, throw it to the ground to death, and then force the young woman to satisfy their lust. Corpses were scattered along the way, and it was a shocking sight. Abandoned babies were crying everywhere, and the sound of refugees filled the fields. While speaking, tears streamed down their faces. The representatives of the Red Swastika Society comforted them and informed the association representatives that they had sent a special commissioner, Wang Guxuan, to Yingfu to investigate and provide relief. Only then did they leave. However, the disaster area is vast, the number of disaster victims is large, and the refugees have not yet returned home. A small amount of money will not help. We sincerely hope that all charity groups will rise up to rescue them.

The Zhejiang Public Association Submits a Document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government 137

Requesting Changes in the Land Survey Method

And Suspending the Collection of Surveying Fees

The Zhejiang Public Association submitted a document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government, stating: To the Zhejiang Provincial Government: Land consolidation should begin with land surveying. Zhejiang Province's land tax follows the old system of the Ming and Qing dynasties. Since the Taiping Rebellion, many fish-scale registers in various counties have been scattered and lost. In the past century, there have been changes in rivers and waterways, siltation and erosion of sand, and reforms in military and garrison colonies, the construction of railways and highways, the amount of land has long been lost, the taxes only have a false name, the tax is not entirely based on the land, and the grain is not transferred with the household. It is not only the wealthy and cunning people who have encroached and concealed land. Land surveying is indeed a matter that cannot be delayed. However, recently, when people from Zhejiang come to Shanghai and talk about land surveying, they are terrified. This is not unfounded moaning, but because the land surveying plan has flaws. Now, let's mention two points: (I) Land surveying expenses should not be charged to the people first. Recently, the Finance Department has been handling the land parcel maps, and the expenses are paid from the old tax items collected from the 16th to 19th years, and the people have no objections. Now it is heard that the surveying expenses are set at 5 jiao of silver per mu, and the Finance Departments have instructed the counties to collect the surveying fees in advance. Thus, the Jiaxing County Government decided to collect 2 jiao of silver per mu first. Those less than one mu will be counted as one mu. If the fees are collected in this way, even small farmers will have to pay several yuan of silver. In recent years, silkworm farming has failed and rice prices have plummeted. How can the farmers who have been in trouble for a long time bear this huge burden? Moreover, before the land surveying has started, the farmers are asked to pay money first, which is similar to extortion. This association believes that it is not possible. It is found that in the 18th year, when the land declaration was carried out, 1 jiao and 2 fen of silver were collected per mu, and the province could collect several million. In the 19th year, the land consolidation fee was collected, with 3 jiao of silver attached to each liang of land tax and each dan of subsidies, which is also not a small amount. The purpose of these two items is to organize the land. The provincial government should first allocate them to be used for land surveying. It is reasonable to take it from the people if it is not enough. It should be ordered to stop the collection of land surveying fees in various counties to relieve the people's difficulties. (II) The land surveying method must consider the people's strength. This time, the land surveying is carried out using the large and small angle surveying, extending the use of technical personnel, purchasing application equipment, which requires a lot of expenses. It is heard that Hangzhou City and County first carried out land surveying, with the help of the Finance Departments, borrowing 1 million yuan of commercial loans, but it has not been completed yet. By analogy, each county will average 500,000 yuan, and the province will need a total of 37.5 million. At this time of poverty, how can we get this huge amount of money? If the expenses are not enough, it will inevitably be abandoned halfway. Land consolidation, the old method uses bow and arrow, and the new method uses aircraft surveying, or large triangle surveying, or triangle root surveying. If you want to be accurate, the new method is better, but the old method of using bow and arrow can also achieve the same effect as surveying if you are serious. The cost can be saved tenfold. A few years ago, Tongxiang County spent more than 40,000 yuan on land surveying, and Huangyan County is also said to be the same. If the surveying is clear, the old method can still be used. If the surveying is not clear, the new method will also lose its effect. The old method can be fraudulent, and the new method is not necessarily not fraudulent. Why must we use large triangle surveying, so that the provincial treasury and the people's strength cannot bear it? Now, the Finance Departments have organized the land parcel maps, and the counties have gradually completed them, which is enough for the surveying. The surveying can also get relatively accurate results. It should be requested to change the land surveying method, reduce expenses, and care for the people's strength. In addition to the surveying personnel, the organization of the land surveying office in each county has provincial instructors, office directors, general affairs team leaders, team members, assistants, etc., with salaries ranging from 180 yuan to 56 yuan. In addition, the salary of the surveying personnel and the expenses are very large, and the organization should also be reduced and the expenses reduced. The above-mentioned points have been approved by the general meeting of members of this association. It should be requested that the government should approve, adopt, and implement it, which is convenient for the public. Sincerely, the Shanghai Zhejiang Public Association.

The Two Railways Stipulate the Collection Method of Loading and Unloading Fees 139

The Loading and Unloading Fees are Added to the Freight Ticket and Collected by the Railways

The Transportation Department of the Jinghu and Huhu-Ningpo Railway Administration, in order to standardize the collection method of loading and unloading fees for intermodal freight, specially issued a letter to the relevant parties, saying: In order to standardize the collection procedures of loading and unloading fees for freight at various stations of the two railways, the methods are different due to the different situations of each station. It is now stipulated that all loading and unloading fees for freight intermodal between the two railways and the Jinpu Railway or the Hangjiang Railway shall be added to the freight ticket and collected by the railways. For example, for "prepaid" freight tickets, the originating station shall calculate and collect them together. For "collect on delivery" freight tickets, the destination station shall calculate and collect them together and submit them to the accounting office. At the end of the month (the stations that have already submitted reports on a ten-day basis may still handle them on a ten-day basis), the station shall issue a bill for the loading or unloading fees that should be obtained and submit it to this department for review and transfer to the accounting office for verification, and then directly allocate it to unify the system. As for the freight transportation of this railway and the loading and unloading fees for the intermodal freight of the two railways, the previous practices shall be temporarily followed.

The Fifteen-Year Savings Plan of the Tongyuan Bank 140

Since its opening, the Tongyuan Commercial Savings Bank on Tianjin Road has been very prosperous in its business. The business of commercial transactions, mortgage loans, and exchange of various ports has been thriving, especially the savings part, which has been developing rapidly. This is because the department handles various savings with simple procedures and generous interest rates, so it is very popular among all sectors. Recently, it has created a fifteen-year savings plan, saving 17 yuan, 4 jiao, and 1 fen per month. When the fifteen-year period expires, you can get 82 yuan, 5 jiao, and 9 fen per month. From then on, you can withdraw forever from generation to generation. Such a one-time savings plan is still a novelty in Shanghai.

The New Ambulance Regulations of the French Municipal Council 141

The French Concession Municipal Council in Shanghai recently promulgated the ambulance regulations, which are recorded as follows: Article 1. The Council has an ambulance for transporting residents who have infectious diseases and want to enter their own chosen hospital (within the scope of Shanghai). Article 2. Anyone who wants to request transportation of a patient with a non-infectious disease, whether day or night, can send a letter to the Fire Department at 193 Xiafei Road or call 80079 or 00 to call the French ambulance. Article 3. When requesting to dispatch a car, you should explain in detail: (I) the name of the requester, (II) the name of the patient, (III) the exact address of the patient, (IV) where to send it, (V) the name and address of the person who recognizes and pays the fare. Article 4. There is always a nurse accompanying the ambulance. If the patient's relatives or friends are willing to accompany the patient to the hospital, they must not make excuses to request to ride the ambulance back to the apartment at any time. Article 5. The ambulance should return to the fire department immediately after sending the patient to the hospital. Article 6. The fixed fare is: residents in the French Concession, 3 yuan per hour or less, 1 yuan for every 20 minutes after one hour; residents outside the French Concession, 4 yuan per hour or less, 1 yuan and 2 jiao for every 20 minutes after one hour. Article 7. If the ambulance is called for no reason, the caller shall pay the above train fare according to the regulations.

Another Korean Political Assassination in the Lixin Lane of Dixiwei Road 142

The Deceased, Liu Yinfa, Was a Core Pro-Japanese Figure

The Murderer Escaped the Scene and is Being Sought by All Parties

At 6:05 yesterday morning, an assassination case occurred in No. 32 Lixin Lane, Dixiwei Road in this port. The injured was a Korean named Liu Yinfa, a core pro-Japanese figure among the Koreans in Shanghai. This assassination is clearly related to politics. The investigation results are recorded as follows:

Circumstances of the Assassination 143

Liu Yinfa, a 35-year-old Korean, lived at No. 32 Lixin Lane, Dixiwei Road. He had a chauffeur-driven car for his commutes. Liu had a wife and four children, and his family was quite wealthy. Liu was the chairman of the Korean Friendship Association, which was composed of a portion of Koreans in Shanghai. In the past, he and the late Yu Guanbin, the owner of the Foci Pharmaceutical Factory who was also assassinated, jointly presided over it. Since Yu's death, all the association affairs were handled by Liu personally. The association is a pro-Japanese organization, and its daily work is quite busy. Liu would go to the association to work every morning at 9:00 AM. Unexpectedly, at about 6:00 yesterday morning, a Korean youth wearing a suit and speaking Japanese knocked on the back door of Liu's residence. When the Chinese maid hired by Liu opened the door and invited him in, the maid saw that she did not know him and wanted to refuse him. At this time, the youth took out a pistol, forbade her from making any noise, and forced her to lead him to Liu's bedroom. The maid was stunned and was forced to go upstairs. The youth rushed into Liu's bedroom. At that time, Liu had already heard the noise downstairs and hurriedly put on his clothes and got out of bed. When he opened the door, the youth took out a pistol and shot Liu six times. Liu fell to the ground in response. His wife woke up in shock and saw her husband bleeding like a spring. She screamed for help in Korean. The youth was anxious and shot Liu's wife again before fleeing downstairs. Fortunately, Liu's wife dodged quickly and only suffered a graze to her lower abdomen. However, she also fell to the ground in extreme pain.

Sent to the Hospital for Treatment 144

Afterwards, the maid downstairs and Liu's coachman, A Er, a Jiangbei native, heard the gunshots and knew that something had happened. They went upstairs to inspect and saw that the master and mistress had fallen in a pool of blood. However, they were still able to groan. They immediately reported to the police station and the Fifth District Third Police Station, and then sent them by car to the Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road, Haining Road for treatment. The hospital examined them. Liu was shot in four places: one in the left armpit, one in the chest, one in the lower abdomen, and one bullet in the lung that did not penetrate. Liu's wife only suffered a graze to her lower abdomen, so she was discharged after bandaging. Liu underwent surgery and was still conscious. It is said that if his condition does not change today, there should be no danger to his life.

Post-Incident Investigation 145

After the incident, reporters went to Liu's residence to conduct a thorough investigation and discovered a box of business cards bearing the title "Chairman of the Korean Friends Association, hosted by Liu." It was also learned that besides being the current chairman of the Friends Association, Liu had previously served as a member of the Shanghai American Volunteer Group, had resided in Europe and America for a considerable time, and was currently also employed in the electroplating department of the American-owned company. According to the Japanese side, his assassination must have been carried out by anti-Japanese elements among the Koreans residing in Shanghai. Furthermore, the shell casings found in Liu's bedroom were examined and found to be of the same type as the handgun used in the assassination of Yu Guanbin. Currently, the police and local stations are conducting a rigorous investigation. At the same time, the Japanese consulate is taking the successive assassinations very seriously and is also undertaking a careful search for the perpetrators.
