Jealousy and Rivalry: Two Heroes Meet in a Courtyard 146

Launching a Retribution Squad in the Early Hours

Both Parties Sent to Court for Questioning and Judgment

Yang Keming, a native of Ningbo, twenty-eight years old, was fond of frequenting brothels. Since last year, he had formed an inseparable bond with a prostitute (stage name: Yifei Laoqi), real name Feng Xiuzhen, at residence number 6, Fuyu Lane, Yunnan Road. The prostitute, like Yang, was born in Changzhou. The previous evening, Yang again went to the brothel to host a banquet. As the party waned and the lights dimmed, another uninvited guest suddenly barged in. Laoqi immediately led him to another room, treating him with obsequious attentiveness, as this man, named Shi Jinnan, a native of Shaoxing, had an intimate relationship with her. He operated a Hongyuan Paint and Hardware Store on Hankou Road and was clearly a prosperous merchant. That evening, Shi had initially hosted a banquet at someone else's home, and after the gathering dispersed, fueled by lingering alcohol, he specifically visited Laoqi, intending for a private chat. Unexpectedly, the two men encountered each other, leaving Laoqi feeling awkward and uneasy. Fortunately, Yang understood the situation and abandoned his desire to stay, departing hastily. However, at five o'clock the next morning, Yang suddenly led several of his fellow townsmen, including Han Shuiqiao, into the brothel. Seeing Shi still sound asleep in the room, he felt a surge of jealousy. With a furious roar, Yang woke Shi. Wielding a written agreement in one hand and raising his fist in the other, he sternly rebuked Shi: "Who are you? How dare you sleep with my fiancée? I have caught you tonight, what do you have to say for yourself? If you resist, my fist may not show mercy!" Shi, hearing this, believed that a prostitute was fair game for anyone, and that staying overnight in a brothel was none of Yang's business. Therefore, he showed no fear of Yang's intimidating behavior. Yang then realized that Shi was not a weakling either. Having embarked on this course, he had no choice but to retrieve an opium smoking set and then go outside to summon Chinese constables from station number 1921. He then accused the brothel of privately hiding smoking paraphernalia and also accused Yang and Laoqi of sleeping together, both violations of brothel regulations, requesting the constables to investigate. Consequently, both parties were taken to the Old Gate Police Station. Under questioning by the police chief, Yang claimed that Laoqi was his fiancée and was ordered to provide evidence. Yang then presented the written agreement he held, which stated: "Agreement: Male, Yang Keming; Female, Feng Xiuzhen. Due to mutual affection, both parties agree to enter into a lifelong commitment. A formal marriage ceremony will be held at the end of this year. Both parties must fulfill this agreement. If the male party reneges, he will compensate the female party with 2,000 yuan. If the female party reneges, she will compensate the male party with 2,000 yuan. Currently, the female party works as a courtesan in a brothel and is not allowed to entertain other guests. If she entertains other guests, she will also compensate according to the above amount. To prevent future disputes, this agreement is made, each party holding a copy for record. July [day missing], 22nd year. Witnessed by lawyer Cao Lin." An investigator, Feng Xiushan, was dispatched to inquire with lawyer Cao Lin. According to Cao Lin, Yang Keming had requested him to witness the agreement, but he had not seen Feng Xiuzhen in person, nor did he know whether Feng agreed to it. The police chief, believing that Cao Lin could not vouch for the validity of the agreement, concluded that Yang had fabricated the document with the intention of fraud and extortion, and immediately detained him as well. Yesterday morning, both were handed over to the First Special District Local Court, where Judge Qian Hongye conducted the preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, presented the case, stating that the defendant Yang Keming had been sentenced to six months in prison at the age of eighteen for forging documents, and had recently been sentenced to one month in prison for theft in the French Concession, demonstrating his lack of good character. Judge Qian then questioned the witnesses and ordered both defendants to be held in custody pending a scheduled verdict.

Shanghai Ships Actively Prevent Theft 147

Two Gangs of Pirates Hide in Shanghai and Hong Kong, Plotting to Hijack Ships

Various Shipping Companies Actively Establish Anti-Theft Measures

Recently, the Dapeng pirates are again plotting to hijack merchant ships. One gang has already infiltrated Shanghai, and Shanghai shipping companies have begun taking precautions, paying special attention to passengers and cargo. The situation is described in detail below.

Plotting to Hijack Hong Kong-Shanghai Ships 148

In late July, shipping circles in Shanghai received confidential reports that the Dapeng Bay pirates had split into three groups and departed to hijack Nanhua-class ships. This news was soon followed by the Yushun hijacking case. The pirates who hijacked the Yushun have now been apprehended by the Shantou Navy. Recently, this port has received further confidential reports stating that two of the three pirate groups have now been dispatched. One group remains hidden in Hong Kong, plotting to hijack merchant ships in the South China region, while the other group has infiltrated Shanghai, intending to plunder merchant ships sailing to various ports in the North and South Seas. All shipping companies have been ordered to take strict precautions.

Shanghai Ships Increase Security Checks 149

Shanghai shipping companies, learning from past hijackings like the Yushun, know that pirates often disguise themselves as northern merchants to board the ships. Since the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in Shanghai implemented passenger screening before boarding, other shipping companies are now following suit to ensure the safety of travelers. Recently, they have taken further steps, requiring all passengers booked via Huangyutou to provide a guarantor. Those without a reliable guarantor or deemed suspicious are not sold tickets. As a result, the safety of sea passengers has been further enhanced.

Suspension of Gold and Silver Transport 150

To ensure maritime safety and fundamentally eliminate any pirate incentives, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has taken the lead in refusing to transport large sums of cash for banks and firms. Recently, various ports have been transporting silver ingots and other valuables into Shanghai.

New Building at the North Railway Station Completed; Traffic Department Began Moving in Yesterday 151

General Affairs Section and Business Section Scheduled to Move Today

Traffic Department to Simultaneously Implement Organizational Changes

The rebuilding of the new building at the North Railway Station of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways has been completed. This has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, the Traffic Department began sorting through documents in preparation for moving in, and the Business and General Affairs Sections are also scheduled to move in and begin operations today. The Traffic Department will also implement organizational changes after moving in, as ordered. Details are provided below.

Beginning the Move 152

Before the January 28th Incident, the Traffic Departments of both railways operated at the North Railway Station. After the North Railway Station was destroyed, they temporarily set up simple offices near the Boundary Road Station. Director Zheng Baozhao, seeing that the new site has been completed, ordered his staff yesterday to sort through documents and begin moving into the new site. In addition to most of the Traffic Department Director's office having been moved, the Deputy Director's office will be moved today. Furthermore, the Business and General Affairs Sections offices are also preparing to move in simultaneously today. Station affairs inspectors, the telegraph room, and the China Travel Service also completed their installation yesterday, and it is expected that the complete move will be completed in the next few days.

Organizational Changes 153

At the same time, the Traffic Department will implement organizational changes as ordered by the Ministry. The department's internal structure was originally divided into three sections: Documentation, Dispatching, and Business. The Documentation Section will now be renamed the General Affairs Section, and the original four divisions of Documentation, Personnel, General Affairs, and Archives will be reorganized into three divisions: Literary Affairs, Personnel Affairs, and Administrative Affairs. The original Archives division will be merged into the Literary Affairs division, and the General Affairs division will be renamed Administrative Affairs, in order to coordinate the various links in the general administrative system. The Dispatching Section, which manages railway transport affairs for both lines, will be uniformly referred to as the Transportation Section. To align with the names of other lines, it will be renamed the Transportation Section. The section's original four divisions of Beijing-Shanghai Train Dispatching, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Train Dispatching, Traffic Control, and Traffic Statistics will be reorganized into three divisions: Literary Affairs, Dispatching, and Traffic Control. The Business Section, which manages railway business affairs, will be renamed the Business Section, and the original four divisions of Passenger and Freight, Public Transport, Investigation, and Business Statistics, as well as the Catering Business Office, will be reorganized into six divisions: Literary Affairs, Passenger Transport, Freight Transport, Compilation and Investigation, Public Relations, and Catering. The original Passenger and Freight division and Public Transport division will be merged into the Passenger Transport and Freight Transport divisions, and the Investigation and Business Statistics divisions will be merged into the Compilation and Investigation division. The Traffic Department has already implemented the above measures.

Ministry of Communications Launches Domestic Social Telegrams 154

Chinese Plaintext at Two Cents per Character

New Year's Telegrams Officially Abolished

To reduce the cost of condolence telegrams for the people, the Telegraph Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications has formulated a type of social telegram, charging only two cents per character within the province and four cents per character outside the province. Shanghai has ordered the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau to comply. The details are as follows.

Telegram Regulations 155

(Article 1) Domestic telegrams (hereinafter referred to as social telegrams) exchanged between various locations within the country (including Hong Kong) that comply with the provisions of these regulations may be treated as domestic social telegrams and charged at a specific rate. (Article 2) Social telegrams are only allowed to be written in Chinese or English plaintext, and the wording within the text is limited to matters relating solely to the following: (A) Congratulations on the New Year, Christmas, marriage, birth of a child, birthday, opening, or move; (B) Condolences, funerals, condolences, disasters, or illnesses; (C) Thank you for the above congratulations or condolences. (Article 3) The fee-paid mark "SLT" must be added before the recipient's name and address on the social telegram, counted as one character for billing purposes. (Article 4) Chinese social telegrams have a minimum charge of ten characters. Telegrams that do not meet the minimum number of characters will be charged for the minimum number. Characters exceeding this will be charged per character. (Article 5) Social telegrams will be charged according to the following specific rates: A. Within the province, Chinese plaintext costs two cents per character, and English plaintext costs eight cents per character. (Article 6) Social telegrams will be delivered and delivered in the same way as ordinary telegrams and news telegrams. (Article 7) All special telegram delivery methods, except for prepaid return fees, telegram bureau or station retention, and forwarding, are not applicable to social telegrams. (Article 8) These regulations do not apply to domestic telegrams exchanged between various locations that are transmitted via the Yantai-Dalian submarine cable, the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable, or foreign lines, or to domestic telegrams exchanged between various locations and Hong Kong that are transmitted via wireless or submarine cable. (Article 9) The Ministry of Communications may amend these regulations at any time if there are any unfulfilled matters. (Article 10) The effective date of these regulations will be determined by the Ministry's order.

Scheduled Implementation 156

The order has been previously received by the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau. According to Mr. Huashi, the Business Director of the Bureau, he told the Huadong News Agency reporter yesterday that after receiving the order, the Bureau has requested instructions from the Ministry of Communications authorities as to whether this method is applicable to foreign telegrams. It is also reported that these telegrams are scheduled to be implemented on the first of next month (September). In addition, after the implementation of this social telegram, all domestic New Year's telegram regulations promulgated on October 24th of last year will be abolished at the same time.

National Silk Exhibition Closes This Afternoon 157

Chamber of Commerce Notifies Various Trades to Participate

Distribution of Certificates and Gifts

The Chinese National Silk Exhibition, jointly organized by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Silk Industry Bank, the Silk Industry Association, and the Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association, has now come to a close. The closing ceremony will be held at 1 p.m. today at the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Representatives from the Party and government agencies have been invited to deliver speeches. Someone Threw a Hand Grenade into Jiu Yi Hosiery Shop Last Night 158

Jiu Yi Hosiery Shop Wholesale Department, located at 1343-136 Rue du Consulat, French Concession, has reportedly been established for seven or eight years. It also has a large-scale factory on Avenue des Soeurs, and its business is very prosperous. However, at 7:25 p.m. last night, just after the employees had finished their dinner, someone suddenly threw a hand grenade from the middle of the road. A loud explosion shook the neighborhood, destroying two large glass windows and two small glass windows on the east side of the shop. Fortunately, all the people inside were standing far away, so no one was injured. The grenade thrower escaped without a trace. The manager of the shop, Wang Liwei, a native of Zhenjiang, reported the incident to the Louza Police Station. The police chief immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate. After inspecting the scene, they collected the remains of the exploded grenade and stored it at the police station pending investigation.

Attended by 200 People Including Kong Xiangxi and Wu Tiecheng

Elected Wang Xiaolai and Eight Others as Preparatory Committee Members

The China Child Welfare Association held its biannual general meeting at 5 p.m. yesterday in the Sun Yat-sen Hall of its headquarters on Museum Road. Over 200 people attended, including Kong Xiangxi, Wu Tiecheng, and Zhang Zhijiang. The meeting was chaired by Kong Xiangxi and passed important proposals such as convening a meeting of leaders of child welfare organizations. Details are as follows.

Attendees 160

Those attending yesterday included Kong Xiangxi, President of the Central Bank; Wu Tiecheng, Mayor; Li Tingan, Director of the Bureau of Health; Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau; Zhang Tingrong, Director of the Information Office of the Municipal Government; Mao Xiaxuan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Jin Gong, District Head of the Fifth District; Zhang Zhijiang; Wu Xingya; Wang Xiaolai; Lin Kanghou; Wu Weide; Sun Ruihuang; Li Zhaohuan; Zhao Jinqing; Gao Fengchi; Qian Zhenya; Wu Zhijian; Wang Wanbai; Wu Liguo; Chen Jingsheng; Pan Shilin; Madam Hua Jingzhen; Madam Ding Shujing; Madam Liu Wang Liming; Madam Li Guanfang; Madam Liu Jinfang; Madam Hua Meijie; Madam Wang Aitian; Madam Wang [name missing]; Xu Jianping; Wang Guanyi; Chen Zhengfan; Zhang Yueru; Zhao Weitian; Ding Bingnan; Gu Yunqiao; Ding Zhixiu; Huang Zhenyong; and over 200 others.

Chairman's Report 161

After formal greetings, Chairman Kong Xiangxi reported, stating briefly: "Today is the day of our China Child Welfare Association's biannual general meeting. The sunshine is so bright, and the weather is so clear, truly enough to inspire our spirit, and to carry out various meaningful and valuable work with an optimistic attitude. Today, I am honored to have all of you enthusiastic comrades, regardless of hardship, take the time to come and participate in the discussion, promote various matters of the Association, and thereby promote the progress of our country. This is truly a happy thing, and it is something I should first of all solemnly thank you comrades on behalf of the Association. Every half year that the China Child Welfare Association goes through, it always has a special atmosphere, so at each biannual general meeting, we cannot help but have special thoughts. In the past six months, the Association has led the country in holding the Second Children's Day, printing and sending approximately 30,000 copies of Children's Day handbooks and other special publications, holding a grand Child Welfare Dance to expand Child Welfare publicity, holding fifteen Children's Protection Lectures, investigating forty-nine cases of child abuse, distributing 10,000 copies of pamphlets advising against child abuse, and adopting one hundred and six helpless children, of whom twenty-five have been entrusted for placement. We have also promoted health knowledge to impoverished families 229 times, sent 4,230 sick children for treatment, assisted in infant health competitions and hygiene campaigns in various locations, and established child welfare groups in the nature of nurseries, housing and caring for thirty infants, providing them with appropriate education. In addition to the above-mentioned routine developments, there are also several special developments, such as (1) proceeding with the establishment of the Beijing Child Welfare Association, which is nearing completion; (2) petitioning the Legislative Yuan to enact children's laws and establish children's courts; (3) publishing the Modern Parents Monthly, promoting parenting education, which has now been published to Volume 1, Issue 4, with many subscribers and very popular among people in society; (4) specially dispatching Deputy Secretary-General Chen Tiesheng to Beiping to handle relief affairs in the North China war zone, contacting more than fifty agencies and organizations, and serving more than 300,000 displaced women and children; (5) expanding the scope of child welfare groups, hiring more teachers, and establishing infant and toddler sections, increasing the original number of infants cared for from thirty to forty. All of these

Page 22

developments are, on the one hand, due to the efforts of the people of the Association, and on the other hand, rely especially on the sympathy and enthusiastic support of the general public. For several years, due to the Association's continued and constant publicity, the general public has also suddenly realized the importance of child welfare work, cooperating closely with the Association in all aspects. In addition to this, the Chinese publishing industry is now also paying great attention to children's reading materials, striving for perfection. Various valuable daily newspapers have also opened special columns to discuss various issues related to children and parents. In Shanghai, due to the initiative of the Municipal Government's Education Bureau and Social Affairs Bureau, the Children's Welfare Committee has been formally established to plan for the welfare of children throughout the city. The Shanghai Morning Post recently held an Infant Health Competition, a Family Fun Day, and a Family Economics Forum, and has also decided to hold a National Children's Health and Beauty Competition on Double Tenth Day this year. From this, it can be seen that there are now more than just a few of us who know the importance of children's welfare in today's society, and that there are also more than just the China Child Welfare Association who are working hard to promote children's welfare. This is truly a gratifying and congratulatory phenomenon, which can be celebrated for the future of China. (7) Not long ago, I made a trip around the world. In this global recession, the people of all countries (especially the people of Germany, Italy, and Soviet Russia) are all tightening their belts, living frugally, enduring hardship, and regarding the country's pain as their own pain, the country's happiness as their own happiness, forgetting the interests of the individual, and striving for the public society, seeking to break through the current economic difficulties. This kind of spirit of public service and dedication to the country is truly worthy of singing, weeping, sighing, and praising. Looking back at the current situation in our country, what is it like, and what is the spirit shown by the people? Regarding this level, you all know it very clearly, and there is no need for me to say more. I believe that the spirit of the people of Europe and America striving for the public is absolutely not accidental, but is the result of long-term training and the long-term cultivation of family education before it can be successfully cultivated. Therefore, in this era of national destruction, internal and external troubles, I hope that the people of our motherland can shoulder the responsibility of saving the country, shoulder the responsibility of training children, and, regardless of whether they are adults or children, can embrace the goal of sacrificing for the country and strive forward, regarding the country's pain as their own pain, the country's happiness as their own happiness, and use this spirit of serving the public and striving for the public to build a strong China, a progressive China, a modern China, and a China that can hold its head high in the world. That is my greatest hope. The future direction of efforts for the China Child Welfare Association and all those who pay attention to the welfare of children will probably be no more than this." After Kong's report, Secretary-General Xu Jianping reported on the association's affairs, and accountant Lin Kanghou reported on the financial situation.

Mayor's Admonition 162

Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave an admonitory speech, stating briefly, "Child welfare is the basic work of saving the country, and the life-sustaining medicine for the revival of the nation. Today's China must rest and recuperate, teach and train, and endure hardship before it can achieve prosperity. From the perspective of the great history of our Chinese nation in the past, if the people of the whole country can recognize the importance of child welfare and work together to train today's children to be healthy citizens in the future, then the great revival of the nation can be expected soon. I hope that the Child Welfare Association will always adhere to this purpose and work hard to do it, then the future of the Republic of China and the future of the Child Welfare Association are both immeasurable."

At the end, photos were taken, refreshments were served, and the meeting adjourned.

Pitiful Prostitute Dies from Abortion 166

At approximately 3 AM yesterday morning, in front of the Guangren Hospital on Avenue Edward VII, a Suzhou woman, Chen Gao, residing at No. 275 North Jiangxi Road, accompanied a 19-year-old Suzhou girl, Chen Danaan, to the hospital, claiming the girl was injured in her lower body due to an abortion and requesting treatment. After examination by the doctor, it was found that Chen's vulva was swollen, inflamed, and necrotic. A surgical procedure was performed, and a pig bone, approximately five inches long and covered in blood, was extracted from the vulva. The girl cried out in extreme pain and was in a dying state.

She lingered until 11:30 AM the following day, when she breathed her last and returned to the underworld. The hospital notified the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched Detective Zhang Desheng to investigate. The girl's body was taken to the coroner's office on Fielun Road. Chen Gao was arrested and, yesterday morning, was escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Wu Ze questioned her. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the police station stated that after investigation, the defendant operated a brothel and bought the girl for 270 yuan to engage in prostitution. As a result, she became pregnant after receiving clients for many months. This pregnancy was an impediment to receiving clients and going to parties. Therefore, a week ago, she asked someone to perform an abortion, inserting a five-inch pig bone into her lower body to cause the fetus to rot into blood. The abortionist's skills were poor, causing internal damage. The pig bone was sucked in and could not be removed, gradually leading to a dangerous condition. That is why she was sent to the hospital for treatment. However, the illness was too advanced, and although the doctor removed the pig bone, it was impossible to save her. He requested a lawful inquiry. Questioned by Judge Wu, Chen Gao stated she lived in the kitchen of the premises and had previously worked as a maid for a Mr. So-and-so on Wuchang Road for a monthly salary of six yuan, quitting after only twenty days. Chen Danaan was her younger sister, living on the mezzanine of No. 293 Wuchang Road. Her parents were deceased, and she was not yet married. On the evening of the 21st, Chen Danaan and a certain woman came to her house, asking her to perform an abortion. However, seeing the girl frequently complaining of abdominal pain, she realized it was caused by an abortion injury. She denied operating a brothel. Judge Wu ordered her to be remanded in custody for further investigation at a later date. At 11:00 AM, the Special Court commissioned Prosecutor Diao Chengtang to go to the coroner's office with a forensic doctor. They confirmed that the deceased girl, Chen Danaan, had died from an abortion. The body was handed over to her cousin, Li Arong, who signed a statement for the coffin and burial.

Record of Gao Lansheng Case Trial 169

| Rescheduled to September 7th |

Gao Lansheng (aka Gao Agen) of Hangxian County, Zhejiang Province, was arrested on the 23rd of last month by French police detective Rao Puzhe at the Cangzhou Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road, along with his accomplice, Sun Qihai of Chuansha, and brought back to the police station. They were sent to the Second District Court for investigation and detention, as reported in previous newspapers. Subsequently, Xu Changrong, who was related to Gao, was transferred from the First Special District Court to the case and sent to the court to await a joint trial. Yesterday was the scheduled trial date. The defense lawyers hired by the defendants, Wang Shizong, Jiang Yiping, Zhu Dianqing, Ge Zhitan, Wu Linkun, Xu Yannian, Jiang Baoqian, and others, arrived at the court to await instructions. At 11:00 AM, Judge Zhang Chaozuo and Clerk Xu Chenghuang took their seats in the First Court. After first hearing three cases related to the Red Pill Hall brought by the police, the Gao case was heard. Court police escorted the three defendants to stand in the defendant's box. Lawyer Wang Shizong stated that he had initially been appointed by the first defendant, Gao Lansheng, but now requested to withdraw his appointment and serve as the defense lawyer for the second defendant, Sun Qihai. Lawyer Wu Linkun also requested to withdraw his appointment as the second defendant Sun Qihai's lawyer and serve as the first defendant Gao Lansheng's lawyer. Jiang Baoqian also requested to withdraw his appointment as Sun Qihai's defense lawyer. The judge then questioned Gao Lansheng, who stated he was 32 years old, formerly residing at No. 4 Sande Lane on Saipo Sai Road, and had moved to No. 16 Mingde Lane ten days ago after being stabbed. He then questioned Sun Qihai, who stated he was 30 years old, residing at No. 8 Xiafei Lane on Beihai Road, and sometimes went to Guangde, living in the coal mine. Finally, he questioned Xu Changrong, who stated he was 32 years old, residing at No. 423 Tangjiawan, and ran a rice store on Zhao Zhou Road. After the questioning, Police Lawyer Yao Zhaodi stood up and presented the case, stating that the police investigation revealed four counts of criminal activity against the first defendant, Gao Lansheng: Firstly, regarding the defendant's involvement in the murder case with Chang Lao Jiu in the Chinese area, the Shanghai District Court had accepted the case and requested the court's assistance in issuing an arrest warrant. The police were now dropping this charge. Secondly, regarding the gambling case, investigation revealed that the defendant was the leader of a flower club, and he was now being charged under Article 280 of the Criminal Law. Thirdly, regarding the sale of opium substitutes, the police had previously uncovered a red pill manufacturing operation at No. 12, Lane 465 Fuchu Road, and arrested Pan Shiyou and others. They confessed that the defendant had opened it. Since Pan and others were involved in a case in the International Settlement, the Supreme Court ruled that the First Special District Court should try the case. He was now being charged under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. Fourthly, regarding bribery of the police, it was discovered that the defendant had bribed police officers while operating the flower club. The police had suspended the bribed officers. He was now being charged under Article 128, Section 1 of the Criminal Law, and a letter from Wang Tingyu found in the defendant's house was presented as evidence. He also stated that the second defendant, Sun Qihai, was arrested along with the first defendant and found to be jointly operating the flower club with the first defendant. He was now being charged under Article 280 of the Criminal Law. The third defendant, Xu Changrong, had evidence of a flower club found in the Anle Third Hotel, and Zhang Deqing and others were arrested. They confessed that Xu was involved with the flower club, and he was now being charged under Article 280 of the Criminal Law. He requested a lawful trial. The judge asked Gao Lansheng if he understood what the police lawyer had said. He answered that he did. The judge asked, "Did you commit murder in the Chinese area?" He answered, "No." The judge asked, "When did the flower club start?" He answered, "In June last year, Mao Axiang came to me and invested 100 yuan. Wu Shuangfu was also involved, but I don't know anyone else." The judge asked, "When did you stop doing it?" He answered, "In August. I went to Hankou in mid-December and came back at the end of March this year. I went again after about a month." The judge asked, "Did you open the red pill manufacturing operation at No. 12, Lane 645 Fuchu Road?" He answered, "No. I don't know the people who were arrested." The judge asked, "Did you bribe police officers when you were running the flower club?" He answered, "I don't know." The judge asked, "What did you do in the flower club?" He answered, "I only had a small share. I didn't do anything." The judge asked, "Who was the manager?" He answered, "I don't know." The judge asked, "Do you know that the Shanghai District Court is issuing an arrest warrant for you for the murder case?" He answered, "No." The judge asked, "Who is Wang Tingyu?" He answered, "He is a friend who is a compradore selling Chinese ships." The judge asked, "What did Wang Tingyu write to you about?" He answered, "He asked me to buy a rubber tire for a car." The judge gave him the letter to read and asked him to explain its meaning. Gao took the letter and answered, "I can't read. I can't even write my own name. I don't know what the letter means." The judge asked, "Who else was in the flower club?" He answered, "I only know Mao Axiang. I don't know anyone else." The judge ordered the defendants Xu to be removed and asked, "Who is Sun Qihai?" He answered, "A friend." The judge asked, "What does Sun do at your place?" He answered, "He's not at my place. He works in the coal mine." The judge asked, "What does Xu Changrong do?" He answered, "He is a friend. I heard that he is involved in the flower club from Mao Axiang." The judge ordered Gao to be removed and called Sun Qihai to the stand. The judge asked, "What is your relationship with Gao Lansheng?" He answered, "A friend. I work in the coal mine." The judge asked, "When did you meet Gao?" He answered, "In June this year, I went to Gao's house to ask for a share." The judge then read Sun Qihai's confession from the police station admitting to running the flower club and asked if it was correct. He answered, "I didn't say that at the police station." The judge ordered Xu Changrong to the stand. The judge asked, "Do you know Gao Lansheng?" He answered, "Yes, a friend. I met him on the boat from Hankou to Shanghai in March this year. Zhang Deqing introduced Gao to eat rice at my store. He asked me to send money to the bank." The judge asked, "What did you do for Gao when he was running the flower club?" He answered, "I didn't do anything in the flower club." The judge asked, "Do you know what Gao does?" He answered, "I know he does rubber business." The judge asked, "You confessed to running the flower club at the police station?" He answered, "The police asked me to confess based on Zhang Deqing's confession." The judge asked, "What was the 2,686 yuan for?" He answered, "Gao Lansheng asked me to send it to the bank." The judge asked, "Did you continue to send money to the bank for him?" He answered, "I knew he was running the flower club on May 12th, so I broke off contact with him." The judge asked, "You were the bookkeeper in the flower club. How much salary did you get?" He answered, "None. There was no salary." The judge asked, "Do you know Mao Axiang and Wu Shuangfu?" He answered, "I only know their names. I don't know them." The judge called Gao to the stand again. The judge asked, "How much money did Xu Changrong earn in the flower club?" He answered, "Although I have shares, I don't care about the internal affairs." The judge asked, "Did you ask Xu Changrong to send money to the bank?" He answered, "No." The judge asked Xu again, "What did you mean when you said Gao asked you to send money to the bank?" Xu answered, "It was delivered by Gao's clerk. Gao himself is hard to meet." The questioning ended there, as it was already past noon. The judge stated that the case files were not fully collected and the debate could not be opened. The lawyers hired by the defendants requested that the defendants be allowed to post bail pending questioning, but the court did not approve. He then announced that the trial would be rescheduled to September 7th and the defendants were remanded in custody.

Bank of China Inspection Report 172

Sixty-Sixth Inspection

The sixty-sixth inspection report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: The members of this committee and the entrusted accountants, in accordance with the rules of this committee, inspected the issuance of Shanghai Bank of China's own bank and the inter-bank receipt exchange coupon reserve treasury. The sixty-sixth inspection was held at the bank on August 27, 1933, and the director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The inspection results are listed as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 10,612,8958 yuan, including 6,512,3993 yuan issued by the bank itself, 1,844,2141 yuan received by inter-bank branches, and 2,156,1824 yuan received by various bank branches. Except for the portion received by various bank branches, which will be inspected separately in accordance with the original method, this inspection of the inter-bank branch portion is as follows: The amount issued by the bank itself and received by inter-bank branches is 8,256,7134 yuan. The amount of exchange coupon reserve for this inter-bank branch is 8,356,7134 yuan, including 5,647,1903 yuan and 2.3 fen in cash reserve, and 2,709,5230 yuan and 0.77 fen in guarantee reserve. The above two items, with the cash reserve accounting for 60% and the guarantee reserve accounting for 40%, were all checked and found to be accurate. In accordance with Rule 5, this report is formally submitted. August 27, 1932, Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, Wang Yansong and Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Xu Xinliu and Wang Zhixin, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association, Li Jisheng and Chuan Songnian, representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association, Liu Hongyuan and Zheng Boren, representatives of various bank branches, Ye Zuotang, Song Hanzhang, and Wen Zongliang, representatives of the directors and supervisors of the Bank of China, and accountant Wang Zikang.

City News 176

Foci Pharmaceutical Factory Opens its Retail Department Today: Foci Pharmaceutical Factory has newly established a retail department and clinic at No. 39 Xizang Road, both of which will officially open today and begin providing medical services. Lili Branch Passengers Crowd: Lili Automobile Company is a leader in the sea taxi industry, with a large scale and as many as eight branches. The company recently saw that the intersection of Aidoa Road and Xizang Road was thriving, so it established a branch there (next to the Shanghai Moving Company). Since its opening, passengers have found its pricing extremely cheap (one yuan per trip) and its speed fast. Those coming out of the Nanjing Grand Theater, the Circus, or the Great World can take a car from this branch to go home most easily. Therefore, in recent days, the crowding of passengers has created a situation of great demand.

Huazheng Factory Receives Multiple Super Awards: The electric fans, generators, and square-panel electric boards produced by the Huasheng Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Factory in this city are famous at home and abroad and have a good reputation. Over the years, the factory has participated in domestic and foreign exhibitions, and its products have been praised by Chinese and foreign people. Recently, at the Railway Ministry's Exhibition of Goods Along the Route and the Third National Products Exhibition of Zhejiang Province, the factory was requisitioned for display. The Ministry of Railways and the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province specifically awarded super-class awards to encourage it.

New Building Completed for Shanghai Bulb Company Glass Factory: The Shanghai Bulb Company previously felt that the glass factory's houses and stoves were insufficient for development, so the board of directors decided to add two large factory buildings and two stoves. The Central Construction Factory undertook the construction last month. By now, one month has passed, and all the projects have been completely completed. The stoves are currently being built quickly and should be completed soon. It is heard that the factory can produce 15,000 light bulbs per day.

Large-Scale National Cosmetics Company to be Established in This City: Mr. Chen Jianming, who once lived a military life, saw that foreign insults have been pressing on in recent years, and domestic industries have been declining and collapsing. The fact that cosmetics and daily necessities rely heavily on foreign imports, causing the outflow of money to reach tens of millions of yuan per year, is heartbreaking. In view of this, Mr. Chen left his gun and came to implement national salvation through production. He raised huge sums of money to establish the Jinlang National Cosmetics Company on Lauerdong Road in this city. He hired well-known domestic technicians to manufacture various cosmetics and daily necessities using chemical methods, in order to slightly save the drain. It is known that many dignitaries of the National Government have given inscriptions to promote it. It is also heard that the company's internal preparations have been largely completed, and the products will be available to people from all walks of life around the time of the osmanthus fragrance.

The West Branch of the Meili Flower Paper Company Opens Today: The Meili Flower Paper Company at No. 306 Nanjing Road in this city specializes in selling wallpaper from major European and American manufacturers. The quality and color are excellent, and the prices and services are especially low and considerate, so it has been well received by society. The company has established a west branch at No. 641 Nanjing Road (that is, the entrance of Daqingli) today in view of its business development and to facilitate customers. The newest colors have been extensively collected. Welcome to visit.

The Quality of Cishi Realgar is Excellent: Realgar, also known as chicken crest stone and potassium sulfide, is a special product of Cili and Shimen counties in Hunan Province. It is one of the world's famous minerals with many uses. It has strong bactericidal and disinfectant properties. However, the quality of the products sold on the market has been very poor in recent years. This year, the Cishi Realgar Bureau is mining and producing exquisite products, which have been shipped to Han in large quantities. The Han口Commodity Inspection Bureau has verified that the potassium sulfide content ranges from 58% to 82%, with a license as proof. In order to promote sales, the Yunlong Company of Han口is the sole agent, and the prices are unified. The goods are also very authentic, which is very different from the products sold on the market in the past.

Letters to the Editor 178

To the Editor,

Although I have wide social interactions on weekdays, I do not send elegiac couplets for those I do not know or those I know but do not attend the funeral. In the past few years, there have been cases of forged elegiac couplets in my name, published in newspapers, such as the deaths of Soong Tzu-wen's mother and Tan Yankai a few years ago, and Yang Quan this year. I did not send any elegiac couplets, but there were forgeries circulating, confusing public opinion. As for works satirizing current affairs, although I sometimes write them, they are mostly in poetry, and they must be elegant. However, the forgeries are mostly vulgar and absurd. I hope that in the future, all newspapers, large and small, must see my handwriting before publishing my elegiac couplets and poems, so that the authenticity can be distinguished, and others cannot make insinuations.

Sincerely,

Zhang Binglin

August 30th

To the Editor,

The news item published in your newspaper on August 28 regarding the resumption of the market closure in Luodian does not entirely match the facts at the time. I am now writing to request a correction:

1. The two committee members, Liu Shouquan and Chen Jiamo, were representatives sent by the Baoshan County Party Department to Luodian to deal with the market closure incident and were not appointed by County Magistrate Jin.

2. Sun Yingfeng is the executive committee member of the First Direct District Branch of the Baoshan County Party Department. He attended as a representative of the branch on that day and was not a staff member of the branch.

3. In the news, there is a passage: "As for Sun Yingfeng, who has been instigating trouble, considering his father's sentiments, no further discussion will be held." The committee members did not mention this comment that day. It is clear that the reporting is inaccurate and should be corrected.

Sincerely,

The Baoshan County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang

Weather Report 179

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather along the coast here would be cloudy or overcast, with the wind increasing in intensity, coming from the east to northeast. There is a possibility of showers. The weather is extremely bad in the Ryukyu Islands, Miyako Island, and the east-south area due to two typhoons in the Pacific Ocean, one moving north and the other moving northwest. There is a tendency to merge. Their central positions were, at around 6:00 AM this morning, the former had moved to within 120 miles of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude, and the latter had moved to within 120 miles of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 133 degrees east longitude. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 92.8 and the lowest was 75.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 79.9 and the lowest was 71.4.

Educational News

Important News

Ministry of Education Stipulates Matters to be Reported by Specialized Schools 180

The Ministry of Education stipulates the matters to be reported by specialized schools and the dates, and instructs the directly affiliated schools and colleges, as well as notifying the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities:

The matters to be reported by specialized schools and above, and the reporting dates, have been previously listed separately, limiting the provincial specialized schools and above to comply. Now, referring to the previous table, the regulations are re-established as follows:

1. List of new students and transfer students, and their academic qualification certificates (graduation certificates or completion certificates). Those starting in the spring semester must report before March 15, and those starting in the autumn semester must report before October 15.

2. Grade reports of students at all levels must be reported within one month after the end of each semester.

3. A list of all students to be subjected to graduation examinations and examination subjects must be reported three months before the graduation examination.

4. The grade reports of graduating students must be reported within one month after the end of the semester.

5. The academic qualifications, experiences, positions, salaries, full-time or part-time status of teachers and staff, if their term is one academic year or more, must be reported within one month after the start of each academic year; if their term is limited to one semester, must be reported within one month after the start of each semester.

From now on, all national, provincial, and registered private specialized schools and above in the country must comply with the above regulations and report on time without delay. In addition to distribution, the Department hereby orders your department to instruct the provincial and registered private specialized schools and above to comply with this order.

Jiangsu Education Department Reorganizes Liyang Education 181

Director Zhou of the Jiangsu Education Department, in view of the fact that the education in Liyang, this province, has had frequent disputes for many years and has not been able to get on the right track, and that one or two troublemakers in the education sector have been implementing various sabotage plans, will be irreparable if they are not reorganized. It has been decided to select Gui Yinwu, the education director of Peixian, a capable and talented person among the education directors of this province, and propose to the provincial government to transfer him to fill the position of education director of the county, and order him to carry out the intentions of the department's reorganization and work hard to advance. At the same time, County Magistrate Bi of Liyang was summoned to the province to be instructed to assist the new director Gui in implementing the progress. It is heard that there were also major educational disputes in Peixian in the past. Since Director Gui took office, it has gradually been on the right track. It is thought that the education in Liyang will also be able to follow in the footsteps of Peixian and move towards the right path after this measure by the Education Department.

Initial Results of Jiangsu Province's Examination for Sending Students to Europe and America 183

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education conducted an examination at the National Chiao Tung University in Shanghai for publicly funded students to study in Europe and America. Examination committee members thoroughly reviewed all subject papers, calculated scores, and unsealed the anonymized papers. A total of seven candidates took the Mechanical Engineering exam, twenty-one for Civil Engineering. One of the Civil Engineering candidates, Zhao Suizhang, did not complete all specialized subject exams due to physical condition issues, so twenty were actually scored. Three candidates took the Chemical Engineering exam. It is reported that among all subjects, Qian Zhonghan, who took the Mechanical Engineering exam, achieved the highest overall score. Qian is from Wuxi and a graduate of the Electrical Engineering Department of Chiao Tung University. He is highly regarded by teachers and friends at the university and has consistently ranked first in academics and conduct each semester, receiving tuition waivers. The second-highest score was Shen Yixian, a graduate of the University of Hong Kong and currently the Director of Academic Affairs at Shanghai High School. His performance was also exceptional in this examination for educational institution personnel studying abroad. The third-highest score was Li Guozhu, currently teaching at the University of Shanghai. He previously studied in the United States at his own expense and earned a Master's degree in Chemistry from the University of Michigan. This year, he is going to the United States again to study Chemical Engineering and thus has a particular strength in Chemistry subjects. There were many applicants for the Civil Engineering subject, but none achieved outstanding results. The list of admitted students is as follows: Qian Zhonghan, Shen Yixian, Li Guozhu, Zeng Runchen, Shi Zhongqi, Zhang Yousheng, Ye Xuean, Huang Wanli, Zhu Baohua, Zhu Guoxi.

Du Dingyou and Others Propose Establishing a Central Library School 184

Requesting the Government to Allocate a Portion of the Cotton and Wheat Loan

To be Used as School Foundation and Operating Expenses

丨Proposed at the Library Association Annual Meeting丨

The second annual meeting of the Chinese Library Association was held at Tsinghua University in Beiping from the 28th to the 31st of last month. Members from the Beijing and Shanghai areas, including Du Dingyou, Liu Guojun, and Qian Cunxun, traveled to Beiping to participate and proposed the establishment of a Central Library School. The original text is as follows:

Main Proposal: The Association recommends to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education that a portion of the Cotton and Wheat Loan be allocated to establish a Central Library Specialized School in the capital.

Reasons: (1) The government has declared that the Cotton and Wheat Loan will be used for construction. Among construction projects, the most important is to improve the people's knowledge and increase their productive capacity. Libraries are the most effective and economical institutions for promoting and improving the people's knowledge. Therefore, a portion of the Cotton and Wheat Loan should be used for the expenses of running a library specialized school. (2) The library profession is increasingly developing, and there is a shortage of specialized personnel. There is only one library specialized school in the country, the private Boone Library School in Wuchang, which is inconvenient. To promote the library profession, it is necessary to train more specialized personnel. (3) Many provinces, cities, and counties have libraries, but their effectiveness has not been significant, largely due to financial limitations, but also due to the lack of suitable talent. To increase library efficiency, it is necessary to establish more library specialized schools. (4) The capital is the center of national attention, the source of government orders, and the location of many universities, gradually becoming the national cultural center. It is appropriate to concentrate national efforts to promote culture to seek development. Libraries are the most important institutions for promoting culture. Therefore, establishing a library specialized school in the capital is most appropriate. (5) The most important way to promote national construction is to restore the rural economy. Rural construction relies heavily on farmer education. Libraries and farmer education are closely related. Therefore, it is advisable to train more specialized library personnel to promote farmer libraries.

Measures: (1) The Association shall separately submit the proposal to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education and hire experts to organize a Central Library Specialized School Committee to formulate a plan for implementation. (2) A portion of the Cotton and Wheat Loan shall be allocated as the school's foundation and operating expenses. (3) The library specialized school should be established in the capital at the outset to coordinate everything, and then be established in other major cities. Proposers: Du Dingyou, He Rizhang, Liu Guojun, Li Yanting, Liu Chunfu, Qian Cunxun, Wu Ziping.

Official Documents Adopt Simplified Punctuation 185

All Agencies to Implement Starting Today

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order to its affiliated agencies stating: Regarding the Ministry of Education's Order No. 7539, for compliance; regarding the Executive Yuan's Order No. 3510, upon review, the Executive Yuan passed the adoption of simplified punctuation in official documents at its 114th and 117th meetings. All ministries and commissions shall implement starting August 1st, and affiliated agencies of all ministries and commissions shall implement starting September 1st. The record has been made and notified, and the implementation should be carried out on schedule. In addition to separate orders, the relevant measures are copied and issued for compliance and for onward transmission to subordinate units for compliance. Therefore, we are issuing this order along with a copy of the original attachment for compliance and for onward transmission to subordinate units for compliance. We are now attaching its measures as follows: (1) The following punctuation marks shall be used temporarily. It is hoped that the various symbols stipulated in the Ministry of Education's unified official document format for educational institutions will be gradually adopted in the future, including commas, periods, quotation marks, reiteration quotation marks, ellipsis points, proper noun marks, and parentheses, etc. (2) Official documents should be divided into paragraphs according to the meaning of the text. The paragraphing and the writing of quoted original text shall be in accordance with the style stipulated in the Ministry of Education's unified official document format for educational institutions, but the use of symbols is temporarily limited to the above seven types. (3) The terminology used in official documents shall fully adopt the regulations in the Ministry of Education's unified official document format for educational institutions.

This Year's Improvement Plan for Shanghai College of Law and Politics 187

Dean Zhang Zhongdao's Statement

Regarding the recent real situation of the Shanghai College of Law and Politics and its improvement plan for this year, Dean Zhang Zhongdao issued the following statement yesterday: Our college was founded in the 13th year of the Republic (1924) and was originally named Shanghai College of Law and Politics. Since the 19th year of the Republic (1930), after being registered with the Ministry of Education and specially licensed by the Ministry of Justice, the Board of Directors and the school authorities have been diligently working to develop the school's affairs. By today, the scale has gradually taken shape, making it one of the famous institutions of higher learning in Shanghai. Over the past ten years, the total number of graduates from our college

exceeds five thousand people. In the first session of the Higher Civil Service Examination and the first, second, and third sessions of the Judges' Examination, graduates of our college have been selected in each session, numbering about ten people. The number of those selected for the Assessor Qualification Examination is even too numerous to count. Many are serving in the judicial, political, and educational circles domestically and practicing law in various places. Taking Shanghai as an example, in addition to the prosecutors serving in the courts, there are nearly one hundred practicing lawyers. Thus, the contribution of our college in cultivating political and legal talents to the nation and society is not insignificant.

Regarding the debt issue of our college, the outside world is largely unaware of the truth, leading to many rumors. Upon investigation, the only substantiated debt is the advance payment from the construction company Liu Yinsheng, which was resolved through mutual reconciliation in the Shanghai Second Special District Court last year. It was agreed that the college would repay Liu Yinsheng 19,800 taels, with an initial payment of 7,000 yuan made at the end of last year, and the remainder to be paid in three years.

One-sixth of the remaining sum would be paid each year in late June and late December. The first installment of over 3,000 yuan has already been duly paid by the college. In addition, although one or two self-proclaimed creditors have filed lawsuits with the court, they all lack sufficient evidence and their motives are suspicious. To safeguard legal interests, the college can hardly acknowledge them. As for facilities, the most important is the library. Since 1930, our college has added new books to its collection every year, totaling over six or seven thousand yuan annually. In addition to the donations from Board Member Wang Chonghui and the political and legal masterpieces purchased by Dean Zheng from Europe, the total number of Chinese and Western books, including existing ones, exceeds twenty thousand volumes (excluding magazine subscriptions). For an independent college, the collection of books can already be considered considerable. Currently, in addition to using the library fees paid by students to purchase new books, we also plan to raise substantial funds separately to extensively collect and enrich this treasure trove of knowledge.

The second issue is the school building. In recent years, the original school building has become insufficient to accommodate the increasing number of students. Its location near the market is unsuitable for education. Therefore, finding a suitable location to build a new school building is an urgent matter. The Board

of Directors, in view of this, entrusted Yan Shenyu, the Shanghai County Magistrate, this spring to purchase over ninety mu of land in the Beiqiao town area. The Board of Directors has resolved to raise funds for construction and has engaged architect Li Zikan to undertake the design and construction. It is currently in active progress. It is expected that the

new school building can be completed by the end of this year.

Furthermore, regarding academic affairs, in the past, the salaries of full-time faculty members were up to 200 yuan per month, and the hourly wage for part-time faculty was

around 4 yuan. However, full-time faculty members taught a maximum of ten hours per week and were paid for twelve months of the year. Compared to other private universities, the treatment of professors was indeed more than adequate. This academic year, the salaries of faculty members have been further increased. The salaries of full-time professors have increased to over 300 yuan. The total amount of professors' salaries accounts for more than 60% of the total school expenditure. At the same time, efforts have been devoted to revising the curriculum, referring to the examination subjects for higher civil servants and the curriculum arrangements of well-known universities at home and abroad, so as to systematize all courses, and to emphasize domestic teaching materials and instill practical knowledge, so as to cultivate practical talents to meet the needs of society.

Upon investigation, last year, the number of students applying to our college was very enthusiastic, with about eight or nine hundred applicants, of whom about three hundred were admitted. If it were not for the daily reputation of the school, which was able to gain the trust of the general public, how could it have reached this point? Just as the first round of recruitment for this academic year was completed, an order was suddenly received from the Ministry to suspend recruitment. Those who do not know the actual situation of our college may not be without conjecture, resulting in

other misunderstandings. In fact, this temporary suspension of enrollment not only does not harm the future of our college, but also strengthens the determination of the college authorities and promotes the cooperation of seven or eight hundred teachers and students in the whole school. We think that the Ministry of Education will certainly provide assistance to schools that are willing to take responsibility for improvement in the future.

In short, no matter what the environment, our college will adhere to its original intention and work tirelessly. In the shortest possible time, we will strive to achieve balanced progress in both spirit and material aspects. We hope that all sectors of society and wise individuals at home and abroad will give us support in terms of opinions or substance. Then the future of education will be fortunate.

Qian Qinglian, courtesy name Shoubo, is from Kunshan, Jiangsu. In 1931, he graduated from the School of Law of Soochow University with a Bachelor of Laws degree. Chinese Walking Association Resolves to Postpone Public Walking Race 196

Rescheduled to October 29th

The Chinese Walking Association held a committee meeting yesterday (August 30th) at 6:15 PM at Moore Memorial Church. Committee members Shi Youhui, Shi Jinsheng, Zhang Zaocai (representing Zhang Zaojiu), Zhang Zaojiu, and Lu Yutian were present, as well as Wang Zhaoxiang, Zhang Zhihe, Cheng Xuan, Yao Yaying, and enthusiastic walking enthusiast Aijieke. The following resolutions were made:

(1) The previously scheduled public men's and women's races on September 24th are now postponed due to the limited time, the National Games has not yet responded, and the many sports events being held in the city make it difficult to pay attention to the walking races. Furthermore, most of the female participants are students, and they will only begin practicing after school starts, leaving little time. It is certain that they will not achieve good results. Therefore, it is specially rescheduled to October 29th.

(2) The first step for the 50,000-meter race is 13 miles. Practice will begin in September. Members who wish to join the training can register with Lu Yutian at the association. The time is from 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM.

(3) The solicitation for entries that began in June has not yielded impressive results. It has now been decided that the committee will be responsible for continuing the process. The best performer will be awarded a silver cup as encouragement.

(4) Recently, walking and long-distance running athletes have been practicing in busy streets, which obstructs traffic and poses a risk to themselves. The Shanghai Municipal Council Police has notified the association about this. In the future, athletes should walk on quieter roads to avoid danger and facilitate traffic. The association has already notified the team captains and hopes that all athletes will pay attention. It is also reported that Shi Jinsheng, who has won championships in the past, has not fully recovered from boils and carbuncles and is unable to move his arms. As a result, he is willing but unable to help. Our Chinese team may lose a key member in the upcoming International Games.

The list of officials is as follows: Chief Leader: Shen Jing; Secretary-General: Shi She; Judging Committee: Sun Tingfang, He Jiyun, Cao Weizhou; Chief Referee: Dong Chengkang; Referees: Dong Xuelin, Gu Yiru, Zhao Huanxian. The Shanghai Hospital has dispatched an ambulance and many nurses to be on site to provide medical assistance.

World Tennis Queen Mrs. Moody Will Definitely Not Retire 200

Previous Retirement Affected by Illness

Will Rest for Six Months to Prepare for Next Year

(San Francisco, USA, 30th Reuters) World Tennis Queen Mrs. Moody, who gave up the final match against Ms. Jacobs in the US Women's Tennis Open due to illness, issued a statement today saying that she did not intend to give up tennis and announce her retirement. She hopes that she will complete the US Women's Singles Tournament in 1934 next year. Mrs. Moody also said that she does not feel regret for her act of giving up. If Ms. Jacobs were to encounter the same situation, she would have done the same. She will rest for six months to restore her health.

Open Tennis Advanced Singles

Wang Wenzheng Defeats Collaso to Gain Re-match Qualification 203

Wang Defeats Xudeng in Straight Sets in Preliminary Round

Also Defeats Collaso in Straight Sets in Second Round Yesterday

At 4:30 PM yesterday at the China Tennis Field, there was an important tennis match. The participants were Wang Wenzheng and Collaso, who fought a fierce four-set battle in the Rotary Cup final. This time, they met again on a narrow path, competing for a spot in the Open Tennis Advanced Singles quarter-finals. Wang had to avenge his previous defeat, while Collaso had to maintain his previous victory. Therefore, the competition became increasingly intense and fierce. However, few outsiders knew about this match, so the audience was sparse. In the end, Wang gloriously defeated Collaso in straight sets and entered the quarter-final week, avenging his previous defeat. As for Wang's preliminary round against Xudeng, Wang also won in straight sets. The scores are as follows:

6 | | 4

(Preliminary Round) Wang Wenzheng {6 | | 2} Xudeng

6 | | 1

11 | 9

(Second Round) Wang Wenzheng {6 | | 3} Collaso

6 | | 1

The First Set Was Infinitely Variable 204

The competition in the first set was extremely fierce, and the unpredictability of the situation was unprecedented in this season's competition. It caused the few spectators to be apprehensive and nervous. The diagonal long shots and sharp, daring shots of the two players were admirable. In addition, they were both able to reduce mistakes, making the game more rational. Wang Wenzheng was cautious, using both sides of the boundary as targets, and launched fierce attacks from left and right, creating a superior record of five to two games, thinking that he could secure the first set. However, things did not go as expected. Collaso's sudden rise extinguished Wang Wenzheng's arrogance, resulting in an unexpected situation.

Difficult to Distinguish Equal Opponents 205

After the five to two game, Wang lost his serve, making it five to three. Collaso took the serve, making it five to four. It was still thought that Wang Wenzheng could easily win six to four, and the next game was Wang's serve, so the hope of victory was very strong. However, Wang made two consecutive double faults, 0 | 30, the situation was not good, followed by three out-of-bounds shots, and the fourth shot was also out of bounds. Wang lost the game, making it five to five. Collaso served and won forty to fifteen (3 | 1). Wang was able to regain the game, taking a six to five lead. The difference in the situation between gains and losses cannot be measured. If the previous game could be like this, Wang would have ended it with six to four. It is really incomprehensible.

The Situation is Thought-Provoking 206

After six to five, it was Wang's serve again, but Wang lost the game again (slip four), making it six to six again. At the critical moment, Wang could not take the opportunity to win, and easily lost it. This must be said to be his only weakness. In the next game, Collaso won, and Wang fell behind six to seven, with a sense of giving up all his previous efforts. Fortunately, he got the serve, making it seven to seven. Collaso won again, and Wang fell behind seven to eight again. However, Collaso also failed to take the opportunity to advance. Wang won the game with slip four, making it eight to eight, and then took Collaso's serve, taking the lead over Collaso with nine to eight again. Collaso also took Wang's serve, making it nine to nine. In the following two games, the situation became more moderate, and finally he won with eleven to nine. The fortune and misfortune in between are very thought-provoking.

The Next Two Sets Were Easily Won 207

In the first four games of the second set, each lost their serve, after two to two, after Collaso lost his third serve, Wang suddenly won his own serve, taking a four to two lead, and the hope was about to become a reality again. After Collaso won the third game, he lost two games in a row, and Wang ended with six to one again. In the third set, Wang won four games first, Collaso took back one game, and Wang ended with six to one again. In these two sets, Collaso's performance was greatly reduced, and Wang won very easily. In the quarter-final week, Wang will also meet his old opponent Zheng Zhaojia.

Ziyan Cup Table Tennis Championship 209

Registration Starts Today

This year's Ziyan Cup Table Tennis Championship is scheduled to begin in late September. Registration starts today. Any official table tennis team can participate in the competition. The registration locations are the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association and Lian Hong Ji Sporting Goods Company on Sichuan Road. The registration fee is two yuan per team. Each team can have a maximum of ten players, seven players attending the competition, and three reserve players. The competition will adopt the Far Eastern Table Tennis Rules, a single round-robin, five-game, three-win system. Each win earns one point. The team with the most points will be the championship team. The prizes include a silver cup for each champion, which can be kept permanently. The third and fourth place teams will each receive a silver shield. The fifth to tenth place teams, and each team that does not forfeit the competition from beginning to end, will each be awarded a prize flag.

A Brief Overview of Sports in the Philippines by Chen Jinzhi 210

I am the captain of the basketball team of the basketball and track and field expedition team of our school (Nanyang High Commercial School). This time, I traveled to the Philippines and stayed in Manila for more than 25 days. In addition to the competition, I engaged in research. Now I will briefly talk about the sports situation in Manila.

To see whether the sports in a place are developed or not, one should look at the organization of sports associations in that place. Manila has the Philippine Amateur Athletic Federation, which is like the Chinese National Sports Federation in Shanghai. This association is in charge of national sports affairs. Manila also has three major sports associations, which are like the Jiangda Sports Federation in Shanghai. This association is composed of the University of the Philippines, National University, and Santo Tomas University, and is the source of various sports talents in the Philippines. The Manila High School Athletic Association is like the Shanghai Secondary School Athletic Association, and is composed of various middle schools in the Philippines that are famous for sports. Therefore, talents are also emerging in large numbers and have achieved remarkable results. Although the Filipinos are said to have a talent for sports, the Philippine authorities are also very willing to promote them. However, the so-called athletes in the Philippines do not seem to be able to practice hard, probably due to the hot weather. Therefore, there is very little hope for the 10th Far Eastern Games next year. Track and field, swimming, tennis, and baseball seem to be weaker than Japan. Volleyball and football may not be a match for our country. The Filipinos' greatest hope for the championship is only basketball.

In addition to basketball, there is another sport that is most popular and most exciting among Filipinos, which is kicking shuttlecock. People of all ages gather in the streets and alleys, kicking back and forth with their front and rear feet, which makes the audience enjoy it.

The most spirited aspect of Philippine sports is the military drills of various schools. The uniforms are neat, and the discipline is strict, similar to the formal army, unlike our students, who regard military training as child's play.
